This framework accurately interprets spatial intent and generates optimized 3D indoor design, improving productivity, and encouraging nondesigner participation. Evaluations across diverse floor plans and user questionnaires demonstrate effectiveness. An independent LLM evaluator consistently rated participatory layouts higher in user intent alignment, aesthetic coherence, functionality, and circulation. Questionnaire results indicated 77% satisfaction and a clear preference over traditional design software. These findings suggest the framework enhances user-centric communication and fosters more inclusive, effective, and resilient design processes. Project page: https://rsigktyper.github.io/AICodesign/

摘要：在建築室內設計中，常常因為客戶缺乏設計知識而產生溝通不良，而設計師則難以解釋複雜的空間關係，這導致了時間延誤和財務損失。最近在生成佈局工具方面的進展縮小了這一差距，通過自動化3D視覺化來解決問題。然而，現有的方法論存在局限性：基於規則的系統實施硬編碼的空間限制，限制了參與性參與，而數據驅動模型則依賴於大量的訓練數據集。最近的大型語言模型（LLMs）通過自然語言使對空間關係的直觀推理成為可能，從而彌補了這一差距。本研究提出了一個基於LLM的多模態多代理框架，能夠動態地將自然語言描述和圖像轉換為3D設計。專門的代理（參考、空間、互動、評分者）通過提示指南運作，協作解決核心挑戰：代理系統使實時用戶互動成為可能，以便進行迭代的空間細化，而檢索增強生成（RAG）則減少了對數據的依賴，而不需要特定任務的模型訓練。這一框架準確解釋了空間意圖並生成優化的3D室內設計，提高了生產力，並鼓勵非設計師的參與。對不同平面圖和用戶問卷的評估顯示了其有效性。一個獨立的LLM評估者在用戶意圖對齊、美學一致性、功能性和流通性方面，始終對參與式佈局給予更高的評價。問卷結果顯示77%的滿意度，並明顯偏好於傳統設計軟件。這些發現表明該框架增強了以用戶為中心的溝通，並促進了更具包容性、有效性和韌性的設計過程。項目頁面：https://rsigktyper.github.io/AICodesign/

##### **Knowledge Graph Extraction from Biomedical Literature for Alkaptonuria Rare Disease**
2603.15711v1 by Giang Pham, Rebecca Finetti, Caterina Graziani, Bianca Roncaglia, Asma Bendjeddou, Linda Brodo, Sara Brunetti, Moreno Falaschi, Stefano Forti, Silvia Giulia Galfré, Paolo Milazzo, Corrado Priami, Annalisa Santucci, Ottavia Spiga, Alina Sîrbu

Alkaptonuria (AKU) is an ultra-rare autosomal recessive metabolic disorder caused by mutations in the HGD (Homogentisate 1,2-Dioxygenase) gene, leading to a pathological accumulation of homogentisic acid (HGA) in body fluids and tissues. This leads to systemic manifestations, including premature spondyloarthropathy, renal and prostatic stones, and cardiovascular complications. Being ultra-rare, the amount of data related to the disease is limited, both in terms of clinical data and literature. Knowledge graphs (KGs) can help connect the limited knowledge about the disease (basic mechanisms, manifestations and existing therapies) with other knowledge; however, AKU is frequently underrepresented or entirely absent in existing biomedical KGs. In this work, we apply a text-mining methodology based on PubTator3 for large-scale extraction of biomedical relations. We construct two KGs of different sizes, validate them using existing biochemical knowledge and use them to extract genes, diseases and therapies possibly related to AKU. This computational framework reveals the systemic interactions of the disease, its comorbidities, and potential therapeutic targets, demonstrating the efficacy of our approach in analyzing rare metabolic disorders.

摘要：Alkaptonuria (AKU) 是一種超罕見的常染色體隱性代謝疾病，由 HGD (Homogentisate 1,2-Dioxygenase) 基因的突變引起，導致 homogentisic acid (HGA) 在體液和組織中的病理性積累。<lb/>這導致系統性表現，包括早發性脊椎關節病、腎臟和前列腺結石，以及心血管併發症。<lb/>由於其超罕見，與該疾病相關的數據量有限，無論是在臨床數據還是文獻方面。<lb/>知識圖譜 (KGs) 可以幫助將有關該疾病的有限知識（基本機制、表現和現有療法）與其他知識連接起來；然而，AKU 在現有的生物醫學 KGs 中經常被低估或完全缺失。<lb/>在本研究中，我們應用基於 PubTator3 的文本挖掘方法，進行大規模的生物醫學關係提取。<lb/>我們構建了兩個不同大小的 KGs，並使用現有的生化知識對其進行驗證，並用它們來提取可能與 AKU 相關的基因、疾病和療法。<lb/>這一計算框架揭示了該疾病的系統性相互作用、其共病及潛在治療靶點，展示了我們在分析罕見代謝疾病方面方法的有效性。

##### **EmergeNav: Structured Embodied Inference for Zero-Shot Vision-and-Language Navigation in Continuous Environments**
2603.16947v1 by Kun Luo, Xiaoguang Ma

Zero-shot vision-and-language navigation in continuous environments (VLN-CE) remains challenging for modern vision-language models (VLMs). Although these models encode useful semantic priors, their open-ended reasoning does not directly translate into stable long-horizon embodied execution. We argue that the key bottleneck is not missing knowledge alone, but missing an execution structure for organizing instruction following, perceptual grounding, temporal progress, and stage verification. We propose EmergeNav, a zero-shot framework that formulates continuous VLN as structured embodied inference. EmergeNav combines a Plan--Solve--Transition hierarchy for stage-structured execution, GIPE for goal-conditioned perceptual extraction, contrastive dual-memory reasoning for progress grounding, and role-separated Dual-FOV sensing for time-aligned local control and boundary verification. On VLN-CE, EmergeNav achieves strong zero-shot performance using only open-source VLM backbones and no task-specific training, explicit maps, graph search, or waypoint predictors, reaching 30.00 SR with Qwen3-VL-8B and 37.00 SR with Qwen3-VL-32B. These results suggest that explicit execution structure is a key ingredient for turning VLM priors into stable embodied navigation behavior.

摘要：零-shot 視覺與語言導航在連續環境中（VLN-CE）對於現代視覺語言模型（VLMs）仍然具有挑戰性。儘管這些模型編碼了有用的語義先驗，但它們的開放式推理並未直接轉化為穩定的長期具身執行。我們認為關鍵瓶頸不僅是缺乏知識，而是缺乏一個執行結構來組織指令跟隨、感知基礎、時間進展和階段驗證。我們提出了 EmergeNav，一個將連續 VLN 公式化為結構化具身推理的零-shot 框架。EmergeNav 結合了計劃—解決—過渡層次結構以進行階段結構化執行，GIPE 用於目標條件的感知提取，對比雙記憶推理用於進展基礎，以及角色分離的雙視場感知用於時間對齊的本地控制和邊界驗證。在 VLN-CE 上，EmergeNav 僅使用開源 VLM 骨幹，且不進行特定任務的訓練、明確地圖、圖搜尋或路徑點預測，便達到了 30.00 SR（使用 Qwen3-VL-8B）和 37.00 SR（使用 Qwen3-VL-32B）的強大零-shot 表現。這些結果表明，明確的執行結構是將 VLM 先驗轉化為穩定具身導航行為的關鍵成分。

##### **Evolutionary Transfer Learning for Dragonchess**
2603.15297v1 by Jim O'Connor, Annika Hoag, Sarah Goyette, Gary B. Parker

Dragonchess, a three-dimensional chess variant introduced by Gary Gygax, presents unique strategic and computational challenges that make it an ideal environment for studying the transfer of artificial intelligence (AI) heuristics across domains. In this work, we introduce Dragonchess as a novel testbed for AI research and provide an open-source, Python-based game engine for community use. Our research investigates evolutionary transfer learning by adapting heuristic evaluation functions directly from Stockfish, a leading chess engine, and subsequently optimizing them using Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy (CMA-ES). Initial trials showed that direct heuristic transfers were inadequate due to Dragonchess's distinct multi-layer structure and movement rules. However, evolutionary optimization significantly improved AI agent performance, resulting in superior gameplay demonstrated through empirical evaluation in a 50-round Swiss-style tournament. This research establishes the effectiveness of evolutionary methods in adapting heuristic knowledge to structurally complex, previously unexplored game domains.

摘要：Dragonchess，由Gary Gygax引入的三維棋類變體，提出了獨特的策略和計算挑戰，使其成為研究人工智慧（AI）啟發式方法跨領域轉移的理想環境。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們將Dragonchess介紹為一個新穎的AI研究測試平台，並提供一個基於Python的開源遊戲引擎供社群使用。<lb/>我們的研究通過直接從領先的棋類引擎Stockfish調整啟發式評估函數來調查進化轉移學習，並隨後使用協方差矩陣適應進化策略（CMA-ES）進行優化。<lb/>初步試驗顯示，由於Dragonchess獨特的多層結構和移動規則，直接的啟發式轉移是不足的。<lb/>然而，進化優化顯著提高了AI代理的性能，通過在50輪瑞士式錦標賽中的實證評估展示了卓越的遊戲表現。<lb/>這項研究確立了進化方法在將啟發式知識適應於結構複雜、先前未探索的遊戲領域中的有效性。

##### **Datasets for Verb Alternations across Languages: BLM Templates and Data Augmentation Strategies**
2603.15295v1 by Giuseppe Samo, Paola Merlo

Large language models (LLMs) have shown remarkable performance across various sentence-based linguistic phenomena, yet their ability to capture cross-sentence paradigmatic patterns, such as verb alternations, remains underexplored. In this work, we present curated paradigm-based datasets for four languages, designed to probe systematic cross-sentence knowledge of verb alternations (change-of-state and object-drop constructions in English, German and Italian, and Hebrew binyanim). The datasets comprise thousands of the Blackbird Language Matrices (BLMs) problems. The BLM task -- an RPM/ARC-like task devised specifically for language -- is a controlled linguistic puzzle where models must select the sentence that completes a pattern according to syntactic and semantic rules. We introduce three types of templates varying in complexity and apply linguistically-informed data augmentation strategies across synthetic and natural data. We provide simple baseline performance results across English, Italian, German, and Hebrew, that demonstrate the diagnostic usefulness of the datasets.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在各種基於句子的語言現象中表現出卓越的性能，但它們捕捉跨句子範式模式的能力，例如動詞交替，仍然未被充分探索。在這項工作中，我們提出了針對四種語言的精心策劃的範式數據集，旨在探究動詞交替的系統性跨句子知識（英語、德語和意大利語中的狀態變化和物件省略結構，以及希伯來語的binyanim）。這些數據集包含數千個黑鳥語言矩陣（BLMs）問題。BLM任務——一種專門為語言設計的類似RPM/ARC的任務——是一種受控的語言謎題，模型必須根據語法和語義規則選擇完成模式的句子。我們引入了三種類型的模板，複雜性各異，並在合成和自然數據中應用語言學知識驅動的數據增強策略。我們提供了英語、意大利語、德語和希伯來語的簡單基線性能結果，顯示了這些數據集的診斷實用性。

##### **Advancing Multimodal Agent Reasoning with Long-Term Neuro-Symbolic Memory**
2603.15280v1 by Rongjie Jiang, Jianwei Wang, Gengda Zhao, Chengyang Luo, Kai Wang, Wenjie Zhang

Recent advances in large language models have driven the emergence of intelligent agents operating in open-world, multimodal environments. To support long-term reasoning, such agents are typically equipped with external memory systems. However, most existing multimodal agent memories rely primarily on neural representations and vector-based retrieval, which are well-suited for inductive, intuitive reasoning but fundamentally limited in supporting analytical, deductive reasoning critical for real-world decision making. To address this limitation, we propose NS-Mem, a long-term neuro-symbolic memory framework designed to advance multimodal agent reasoning by integrating neural memory with explicit symbolic structures and rules. Specifically, NS-Mem is operated around three core components of a memory system: (1) a three-layer memory architecture that consists episodic layer, semantic layer and logic rule layer, (2) a memory construction and maintenance mechanism implemented by SK-Gen that automatically consolidates structured knowledge from accumulated multimodal experiences and incrementally updates both neural representations and symbolic rules, and (3) a hybrid memory retrieval mechanism that combines similarity-based search with deterministic symbolic query functions to support structured reasoning. Experiments on real-world multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that Neural-Symbolic Memory achieves an average 4.35% improvement in overall reasoning accuracy over pure neural memory systems, with gains of up to 12.5% on constrained reasoning queries, validating the effectiveness of NS-Mem.

摘要：最近在大型語言模型方面的進展推動了智能代理在開放世界的多模態環境中出現。<lb/>為了支持長期推理，這些代理通常配備外部記憶系統。<lb/>然而，大多數現有的多模態代理記憶主要依賴神經表示和基於向量的檢索，這些方法適合於歸納性、直觀性的推理，但在支持分析性、演繹性推理方面根本有限，而這對於現實世界的決策至關重要。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了NS-Mem，一種長期神經符號記憶框架，旨在通過將神經記憶與明確的符號結構和規則相結合來推進多模態代理的推理。<lb/>具體而言，NS-Mem圍繞記憶系統的三個核心組件運作： (1) 一個由情節層、語義層和邏輯規則層組成的三層記憶架構， (2) 由SK-Gen實現的記憶構建和維護機制，自動整合來自累積的多模態經驗的結構化知識並逐步更新神經表示和符號規則，以及 (3) 一種混合記憶檢索機制，結合基於相似性的搜索和確定性符號查詢功能，以支持結構化推理。<lb/>在現實世界的多模態推理基準上的實驗顯示，神經符號記憶在整體推理準確性上比純神經記憶系統平均提高了4.35%，在受限推理查詢上最高提高了12.5%，驗證了NS-Mem的有效性。

##### **SCAN: Sparse Circuit Anchor Interpretable Neuron for Lifelong Knowledge Editing**
2603.15226v1 by Yuhuan Liu, Haitian Zhong, Xinyuan Xia, Qiang Liu, Shu Wu, Liang Wang

Large Language Models (LLMs) often suffer from catastrophic forgetting and collapse during sequential knowledge editing. This vulnerability stems from the prevailing dense editing paradigm, which treats models as black boxes and relies on coarse-grained parameter interventions that inevitably disrupt preserved knowledge. To address this, we propose SCAN (a sparse editing framework based on Sparse Circuit Anchored Neuron) which transforms editing into a mechanism-aware manipulation by constructing a knowledge circuit via Sparse Transcoders. Experiments on Gemma2, Qwen3, and Llama3.1 across CounterFact, ZsRE and WikiFactDiff demonstrate that SCAN achieves a superior performance, maintaining model integrity on benchmarks like MMLU and GSM8K even after 3,000 sequential edits, whereas other existing methods deteriorate progressively as editing accumulates, eventually resulting in model collapse.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在連續知識編輯過程中常常遭受災難性遺忘和崩潰。這種脆弱性源於當前的密集編輯範式，該範式將模型視為黑箱，並依賴於粗粒度的參數干預，這不可避免地破壞了已保存的知識。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了SCAN（基於稀疏電路錨定神經元的稀疏編輯框架），它通過構建知識電路來將編輯轉變為一種機制感知的操作，該電路是通過稀疏轉碼器實現的。在Gemma2、Qwen3和Llama3.1上進行的CounterFact、ZsRE和WikiFactDiff實驗表明，SCAN實現了卓越的性能，即使在經歷3,000次連續編輯後，仍能在MMLU和GSM8K等基準上保持模型的完整性，而其他現有方法隨著編輯的積累逐漸惡化，最終導致模型崩潰。

##### **Bidirectional Chinese and English Passive Sentences Dataset for Machine Translation**
2603.15227v1 by Xinyue Ma, Pol Pastells, Mireia Farrús, Mariona Taulé

Machine Translation (MT) evaluation has gone beyond metrics, towards more specific linguistic phenomena. Regarding English-Chinese language pairs, passive sentences are constructed and distributed differently due to language variation, thus need special attention in MT. This paper proposes a bidirectional multi-domain dataset of passive sentences, extracted from five Chinese-English parallel corpora and annotated automatically with structure labels according to human translation, and a test set with manually verified annotation. The dataset consists of 73,965 parallel sentence pairs (2,358,731 English words, 3,498,229 Chinese characters). We evaluate two state-of-the-art open-source MT systems with our dataset, and four commercial models with the test set. The results show that, unlike humans, models are more influenced by the voice of the source text rather than the general voice usage of the source language, and therefore tend to maintain the passive voice when translating a passive in either direction. However, models demonstrate some knowledge of the low frequency and predominantly negative context of Chinese passives, leading to higher voice consistency with human translators in English-to-Chinese translation than in Chinese-to-English translation. Commercial NMT models scored higher in metric evaluations, but LLMs showed a better ability to use diverse alternative translations. Datasets and annotation script will be shared upon request.

摘要：機器翻譯（MT）評估已經超越了指標，朝向更具體的語言現象。關於英中語言對，因語言變異，被動句的構造和分佈有所不同，因此在機器翻譯中需要特別關注。本文提出了一個雙向多領域的被動句數據集，該數據集從五個中英平行語料庫中提取，並根據人工翻譯自動標註結構標籤，還包括一個經過人工驗證標註的測試集。該數據集包含73,965對平行句子（2,358,731個英語單詞，3,498,229個漢字）。我們使用這個數據集對兩個最先進的開源機器翻譯系統進行評估，並對四個商業模型使用測試集進行評估。結果顯示，與人類不同，模型更受源文本的語態影響，而不是源語言的一般語態使用，因此在翻譯被動句時，無論方向如何，往往傾向於保持被動語態。然而，模型對中文被動語態的低頻率和主要負面語境有一定的認識，這導致在英譯中與人類翻譯者的語態一致性高於中譯英。商業NMT模型在指標評估中得分較高，但LLMs在使用多樣的替代翻譯方面顯示出更好的能力。數據集和標註腳本將根據要求分享。

##### **CATFormer: When Continual Learning Meets Spiking Transformers With Dynamic Thresholds**
2603.15184v1 by Vaishnavi Nagabhushana, Kartikay Agrawal, Ayon Borthakur

Although deep neural networks perform extremely well in controlled environments, they fail in real-world scenarios where data isn't available all at once, and the model must adapt to a new data distribution that may or may not follow the initial distribution. Previously acquired knowledge is lost during subsequent updates based on new data. a phenomenon commonly known as catastrophic forgetting. In contrast, the brain can learn without such catastrophic forgetting, irrespective of the number of tasks it encounters. Existing spiking neural networks (SNNs) for class-incremental learning (CIL) suffer a sharp performance drop as tasks accumulate. We here introduce CATFormer (Context Adaptive Threshold Transformer), a scalable framework that overcomes this limitation. We observe that the key to preventing forgetting in SNNs lies not only in synaptic plasticity but also in modulating neuronal excitability. At the core of CATFormer is the Dynamic Threshold Leaky Integrate-and-Fire (DTLIF) neuron model, which leverages context-adaptive thresholds as the primary mechanism for knowledge retention. This is paired with a Gated Dynamic Head Selection (G-DHS) mechanism for task-agnostic inference. Extensive evaluation on both static (CIFAR-10/100/Tiny-ImageNet) and neuromorphic (CIFAR10-DVS/SHD) datasets reveals that CATFormer outperforms existing rehearsal-free CIL algorithms across various task splits, establishing it as an ideal architecture for energy-efficient, true-class incremental learning.

摘要：儘管深度神經網絡在受控環境中表現極佳，但在現實世界的場景中，它們失敗了，因為數據並不是一次性可用的，模型必須適應一個新的數據分佈，而這個分佈可能遵循或不遵循最初的分佈。基於新數據的後續更新中，先前獲得的知識會喪失，這種現象通常被稱為災難性遺忘。相對而言，大腦可以在不發生這種災難性遺忘的情況下學習，無論它遇到多少任務。現有的用於類別增量學習（CIL）的脈衝神經網絡（SNNs）在任務累積時會遭遇性能急劇下降。我們在此介紹CATFormer（上下文自適應閾值Transformer），這是一個可擴展的框架，克服了這一限制。我們觀察到，防止SNNs遺忘的關鍵不僅在於突觸可塑性，還在於調節神經元的興奮性。CATFormer的核心是動態閾值漏積分發射（DTLIF）神經元模型，它利用上下文自適應閾值作為知識保留的主要機制。這與一種門控動態頭選擇（G-DHS）機制相結合，用於任務無關的推理。對靜態（CIFAR-10/100/Tiny-ImageNet）和神經形態（CIFAR10-DVS/SHD）數據集的廣泛評估顯示，CATFormer在各種任務拆分中超越了現有的無重播CIL算法，確立了它作為能量高效、真實類別增量學習的理想架構。

##### **Multimodal Connectome Fusion via Cross-Attention for Autism Spectrum Disorder Classification Using Graph Learning**
2603.15168v1 by Ansar Rahman, Hassan Shojaee-Mend, Sepideh Hatamikia

Autism spectrum disorder (ASD) is a complex neurodevelopmental condition characterized by atypical functional brain connectivity and subtle structural alterations. rs-fMRI has been widely used to identify disruptions in large-scale brain networks, while structural MRI provides complementary information about morphological organization. Despite their complementary nature, effectively integrating these heterogeneous imaging modalities within a unified framework remains challenging. This study proposes a multimodal graph learning framework that preserves the dominant role of functional connectivity while integrating structural imaging and phenotypic information for ASD classification. The proposed framework is evaluated on ABIDE-I dataset. Each subject is represented as a node within a population graph. Functional and structural features are extracted as modality-specific node attributes, while inter-subject relationships are modeled using a pairwise association encoder (PAE) based on phenotypic information. Two Edge Variational GCNs are trained to learn subject-level embeddings. To enable effective multimodal integration, we introduce a novel asymmetric transformer-based cross-attention mechanism that allows functional embeddings to selectively incorporate complementary structural information while preserving functional dominance. The fused embeddings are then passed to a MLP for ASD classification. Using stratified 10-fold cross-validation, the framework achieved an AUC of 87.3% and an accuracy of 84.4%. Under leave-one-site-out cross-validation (LOSO-CV), the model achieved an average cross-site accuracy of 82.0%, outperforming existing methods by approximately 3% under 10-fold cross-validation and 7% under LOSO-CV. The proposed framework effectively integrates heterogeneous multimodal data from the multi-site ABIDE-I dataset, improving automated ASD classification across imaging sites.

摘要：自閉症譜系障礙（ASD）是一種複雜的神經發展狀況，其特徵是功能性大腦連接的異常和微妙的結構變化。rs-fMRI已被廣泛用於識別大規模大腦網絡中的中斷，而結構性MRI則提供有關形態組織的補充信息。儘管它們具有互補性，但在統一框架內有效整合這些異質成像模態仍然具有挑戰性。本研究提出了一個多模態圖學習框架，該框架在整合結構成像和表型信息以進行ASD分類的同時，保留了功能連接的主導作用。所提出的框架在ABIDE-I數據集上進行評估。每個受試者在一個人口圖中被表示為一個節點。功能性和結構性特徵被提取為模態特定的節點屬性，而受試者之間的關係則使用基於表型信息的成對關聯編碼器（PAE）進行建模。訓練了兩個邊緣變分GCN以學習受試者級別的嵌入。為了實現有效的多模態整合，我們引入了一種新穎的非對稱Transformer基於交叉注意力機制，該機制允許功能嵌入選擇性地融合補充的結構信息，同時保留功能的主導地位。然後將融合的嵌入傳遞給MLP以進行ASD分類。使用分層的10折交叉驗證，該框架達到了87.3%的AUC和84.4%的準確率。在留一站交叉驗證（LOSO-CV）下，該模型達到了82.0%的平均跨站準確率，超過了現有方法在10折交叉驗證下約3%和在LOSO-CV下約7%的表現。所提出的框架有效整合了來自多站點ABIDE-I數據集的異質多模態數據，改善了跨成像站點的自動ASD分類。

##### **To See is Not to Master: Teaching LLMs to Use Private Libraries for Code Generation**
2603.15159v2 by Yitong Zhang, Chengze Li, Ruize Chen, Guowei Yang, Xiaoran Jia, Yijie Ren, Jia Li

Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown strong potential for code generation, yet they remain limited in private-library-oriented code generation, where the goal is to generate code using APIs from private libraries. Existing approaches mainly rely on retrieving private-library API documentation and injecting relevant knowledge into the context at inference time. However, our study shows that this is insufficient: even given accurate required knowledge, LLMs still struggle to invoke private-library APIs effectively.
  To address this limitation, we propose PriCoder, an approach that teaches LLMs to invoke private-library APIs through automatically synthesized data. Specifically, PriCoder models private-library data synthesis as the construction of a graph, and alternates between two graph operators: (1) Progressive Graph Evolution, which improves data diversity by progressively synthesizing more diverse training samples from basic ones, and (2) Multidimensional Graph Pruning, which improves data quality through a rigorous filtering pipeline. To support rigorous evaluation, we construct two new benchmarks based on recently released libraries that are unfamiliar to the tested models. Experiments on three mainstream LLMs show that PriCoder substantially improves private-library-oriented code generation, yielding gains of over 20% in pass@1 in many settings, while causing negligible impact on general code generation capability. Our code and benchmarks are publicly available at https://github.com/eniacode/PriCoder.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在代碼生成方面顯示出強大的潛力，但在以私有庫為導向的代碼生成中仍然有限，該目標是使用私有庫的 API 生成代碼。現有的方法主要依賴於檢索私有庫 API 文檔並在推理時將相關知識注入上下文中。然而，我們的研究顯示這是不夠的：即使提供準確的所需知識，LLMs 在有效調用私有庫 API 時仍然面臨困難。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了 PriCoder，一種通過自動合成數據來教導 LLMs 調用私有庫 API 的方法。具體而言，PriCoder 將私有庫數據合成建模為圖的構建，並在兩個圖操作之間交替進行：（1）逐步圖演化，通過逐步合成更具多樣性的訓練樣本來提高數據多樣性，以及（2）多維圖修剪，通過嚴格的過濾管道來提高數據質量。<lb/>為了支持嚴格的評估，我們基於最近發布的對測試模型不熟悉的庫構建了兩個新的基準。對三個主流 LLM 的實驗顯示，PriCoder 顯著改善了以私有庫為導向的代碼生成，在許多設置中帶來超過 20% 的 pass@1 增益，同時對一般代碼生成能力的影響微乎其微。我們的代碼和基準可在 https://github.com/eniacode/PriCoder 上公開獲取。

##### **MMKU-Bench: A Multimodal Update Benchmark for Diverse Visual Knowledge**
2603.15117v1 by Baochen Fu, Yuntao Du, Cheng Chang, Baihao Jin, Wenzhi Deng, Muhao Xu, Hongmei Yan, Weiye Song, Yi Wan

As real-world knowledge continues to evolve, the parametric knowledge acquired by multimodal models during pretraining becomes increasingly difficult to remain consistent with real-world knowledge. Existing research on multimodal knowledge updating focuses only on learning previously unknown knowledge, while overlooking the need to update knowledge that the model has already mastered but that later changes; moreover, evaluation is limited to the same modality, lacking a systematic analysis of cross-modal consistency. To address these issues, this paper proposes MMKU-Bench, a comprehensive evaluation benchmark for multimodal knowledge updating, which contains over 25k knowledge instances and more than 49k images, covering two scenarios, updated knowledge and unknown knowledge, thereby enabling comparative analysis of learning across different knowledge types. On this benchmark, we evaluate a variety of representative approaches, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), and knowledge editing (KE). Experimental results show that SFT and RLHF are prone to catastrophic forgetting, while KE better preserve general capabilities but exhibit clear limitations in continual updating. Overall, MMKU-Bench provides a reliable and comprehensive evaluation benchmark for multimodal knowledge updating, advancing progress in this field.

摘要：隨著現實世界知識的不斷演變，多模態模型在預訓練期間獲得的參數知識變得越來越難以與現實世界知識保持一致。現有的多模態知識更新研究僅專注於學習先前未知的知識，而忽略了更新模型已經掌握但後來發生變化的知識的需求；此外，評估僅限於相同模態，缺乏對跨模態一致性的系統分析。為了解決這些問題，本文提出了MMKU-Bench，一個針對多模態知識更新的綜合評估基準，該基準包含超過25,000個知識實例和超過49,000張圖片，涵蓋了更新知識和未知知識兩種場景，從而能夠進行不同知識類型之間學習的比較分析。在這個基準上，我們評估了各種具有代表性的方式，包括監督微調（SFT）、來自人類反饋的強化學習（RLHF）和知識編輯（KE）。實驗結果顯示，SFT和RLHF容易發生災難性遺忘，而KE則更好地保留了一般能力，但在持續更新方面顯示出明顯的限制。總體而言，MMKU-Bench提供了一個可靠且全面的多模態知識更新評估基準，推進了該領域的進展。

##### **Open Biomedical Knowledge Graphs at Scale: Construction, Federation, and AI Agent Access with Samyama Graph Database**
2603.15080v2 by Madhulatha Mandarapu, Sandeep Kunkunuru

Biomedical knowledge is fragmented across siloed databases -- Reactome for pathways, STRING for protein interactions, ClinicalTrials.gov for study registries, DrugBank for drug vocabularies, DGIdb for drug-gene interactions, SIDER for side effects. We present three open-source biomedical knowledge graphs -- Pathways KG (118,686 nodes, 834,785 edges from 5 sources), Clinical Trials KG (7,774,446 nodes, 26,973,997 edges from 5 sources), and Drug Interactions KG (32,726 nodes, 191,970 edges from 3 sources) -- built on Samyama, a high-performance graph database written in Rust.
  Our contributions are threefold. First, we describe a reproducible ETL pattern for constructing large-scale KGs from heterogeneous public data sources, with cross-source deduplication, batch loading (Python Cypher and Rust native loaders), and portable snapshot export. Second, we demonstrate cross-KG federation: loading all three snapshots into a single graph tenant enables property-based joins across datasets. Third, we introduce schema-driven MCP server generation for LLM agent access, evaluated on a new BiomedQA benchmark (40 pharmacology questions): domain-specific MCP tools achieve 98% accuracy vs. 0% for text-to-Cypher and 75% for standalone GPT-4o.
  All data sources are open-license. The combined federated graph (7.9M nodes, 28M edges) loads in approximately 3 minutes on commodity cloud hardware, and cross-KG queries complete in 80ms-4s.

摘要：生物醫學知識分散在各個孤立的數據庫中——Reactome 用於途徑，STRING 用於蛋白質互動，ClinicalTrials.gov 用於研究登記，DrugBank 用於藥物詞彙，DGIdb 用於藥物-基因互動，SIDER 用於副作用。我們提出了三個開源生物醫學知識圖——Pathways KG（118,686 個節點，834,785 條邊來自 5 個來源），Clinical Trials KG（7,774,446 個節點，26,973,997 條邊來自 5 個來源），以及 Drug Interactions KG（32,726 個節點，191,970 條邊來自 3 個來源）——這些都是基於 Samyama 建立的，這是一個用 Rust 編寫的高性能圖數據庫。<lb/>
我們的貢獻有三個方面。首先，我們描述了一種可重複的 ETL 模式，用於從異構公共數據源構建大規模知識圖，具有跨源去重、批量加載（Python Cypher 和 Rust 原生加載器）和可攜式快照導出。第二，我們展示了跨知識圖的聯邦：將所有三個快照加載到單一圖租戶中，使得跨數據集的基於屬性的聯接成為可能。第三，我們引入了基於模式的 MCP 伺服器生成，以便 LLM 代理訪問，並在新的 BiomedQA 基準（40 個藥理學問題）上進行評估：領域特定的 MCP 工具達到 98% 的準確率，而文本到 Cypher 的準確率為 0%，獨立 GPT-4o 的準確率為 75%。<lb/>
所有數據源均為開放許可。合併的聯邦圖（7.9M 節點，28M 條邊）在商品雲硬體上加載約需 3 分鐘，跨知識圖查詢的完成時間為 80 毫秒至 4 秒。

##### **Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning**
2603.15054v1 by Ziyu Cheng, Jinsheng Ren, Zhouxian Jiang, Chenzhihang Li, Rongye Shi, Bin Liang, Jun Yang

Effective communication is pivotal for addressing complex collaborative tasks in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). Yet, limited communication bandwidth and dynamic, intricate environmental topologies present significant challenges in identifying high-value communication partners. Agents must consequently select collaborators under uncertainty, lacking a priori knowledge of which partners can deliver task-critical information. To this end, we propose Interference-Aware K-Step Reachable Communication (IA-KRC), a novel framework that enhances cooperation via two core components: (1) a K-Step reachability protocol that confines message passing to physically accessible neighbors, and (2) an interference-prediction module that optimizes partner choice by minimizing interference while maximizing utility. Compared to existing methods, IA-KRC enables substantially more persistent and efficient cooperation despite environmental interference. Comprehensive evaluations confirm that IA-KRC achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art baselines, while demonstrating enhanced robustness and scalability in complex topological and highly dynamic multi-agent scenarios.

摘要：有效的溝通對於解決多智能體強化學習 (MARL) 中的複雜協作任務至關重要。<lb/>然而，有限的通信帶寬和動態、複雜的環境拓撲在識別高價值通信夥伴時帶來了重大挑戰。<lb/>因此，智能體必須在不確定的情況下選擇合作者，缺乏事先知道哪些夥伴可以提供任務關鍵信息的知識。<lb/>為此，我們提出了干擾感知 K 步可達通信 (IA-KRC)，這是一個通過兩個核心組件增強合作的新框架：<lb/>(1) 一個 K 步可達性協議，將消息傳遞限制在物理可接觸的鄰居之間，<lb/>以及 (2) 一個干擾預測模塊，通過最小化干擾同時最大化效用來優化夥伴選擇。<lb/>與現有方法相比，IA-KRC 使得在環境干擾下能夠實現更持久和高效的合作。<lb/>全面的評估證實 IA-KRC 在性能上優於最先進的基準，同時在複雜拓撲和高度動態的多智能體場景中展現出增強的魯棒性和可擴展性。

##### **TrajFlow: Nation-wide Pseudo GPS Trajectory Generation with Flow Matching Models**
2603.15009v1 by Peiran Li, Jiawei Wang, Haoran Zhang, Xiaodan Shi, Noboru Koshizuka, Chihiro Shimizu, Renhe Jiang

The importance of mobile phone GPS trajectory data is widely recognized across many fields, yet the use of real data is often hindered by privacy concerns, limited accessibility, and high acquisition costs. As a result, generating pseudo-GPS trajectory data has become an active area of research. Recent diffusion-based approaches have achieved strong fidelity but remain limited in spatial scale (small urban areas), transportation-mode diversity, and efficiency (requiring numerous sampling steps). To address these challenges, we introduce TrajFlow, which to the best of our knowledge is the first flow-matching-based generative model for GPS trajectory generation. TrajFlow leverages the flow-matching paradigm to improve robustness and efficiency across multiple geospatial scales, and incorporates a trajectory harmonization and reconstruction strategy to jointly address scalability, diversity, and efficiency. Using a nationwide mobile phone GPS dataset with millions of trajectories across Japan, we show that TrajFlow or its variants consistently outperform diffusion-based and deep generative baselines at urban, metropolitan, and nationwide levels. As the first nationwide, multi-scale GPS trajectory generation model, TrajFlow demonstrates strong potential to support inter-region urban planning, traffic management, and disaster response, thereby advancing the resilience and intelligence of future mobility systems.

摘要：手機 GPS 軌跡數據的重要性在許多領域中得到了廣泛認可，然而，實際數據的使用常常受到隱私問題、有限的可獲得性和高昂的獲取成本的阻礙。<lb/>因此，生成偽 GPS 軌跡數據已成為一個活躍的研究領域。<lb/>最近的擴散基礎方法已經實現了強大的真實性，但在空間範圍（小型城市地區）、交通模式多樣性和效率（需要大量取樣步驟）方面仍然有限。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們引入了 TrajFlow，據我們所知，這是第一個基於流匹配的 GPS 軌跡生成生成模型。<lb/>TrajFlow 利用流匹配範式來提高多個地理空間尺度上的穩健性和效率，並結合了一種軌跡協調和重建策略，以共同解決可擴展性、多樣性和效率問題。<lb/>使用一個涵蓋日本數百萬條軌跡的全國手機 GPS 數據集，我們展示了 TrajFlow 或其變體在城市、大都市和全國層面上始終優於基於擴散和深度生成的基準。<lb/>作為第一個全國性、多尺度的 GPS 軌跡生成模型，TrajFlow 展示了支持區域間城市規劃、交通管理和災害應對的強大潛力，從而推進未來移動系統的韌性和智慧。

##### **OrgForge: A Multi-Agent Simulation Framework for Verifiable Synthetic Corporate Corpora**
2603.14997v1 by Jeffrey Flynt

Evaluating retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) pipelines requires corpora where ground truth is knowable, temporally structured, and cross-artifact properties that real-world datasets rarely provide cleanly. Existing resources such as the Enron corpus carry legal ambiguity, demographic skew, and no structured ground truth. Purely LLM-generated synthetic data solves the legal problem but introduces a subtler one: the generating model cannot be prevented from hallucinating facts that contradict themselves across documents.We present OrgForge, an open-source multi-agent simulation framework that enforces a strict physics-cognition boundary: a deterministic Python engine maintains a SimEvent ground truth bus; large language models generate only surface prose, constrained by validated proposals. An actor-local clock enforces causal timestamp correctness across all artifact types, eliminating the class of timeline inconsistencies that arise when timestamps are sampled independently per document. We formalize three graph-dynamic subsystems stress propagation via betweenness centrality, temporal edge-weight decay, and Dijkstra escalation routing that govern organizational behavior independently of any LLM. Running a configurable N-day simulation, OrgForge produces interleaved Slack threads, JIRA tickets, Confluence pages, Git pull requests, and emails, all traceable to a shared, immutable event log. We additionally describe a causal chain tracking subsystem that accumulates cross-artifact evidence graphs per incident, a hybrid reciprocal-rank-fusion recurrence detector for identifying repeated failure classes, and an inbound/outbound email engine that routes vendor alerts, customer complaints, and HR correspondence through gated causal chains with probabilistic drop simulation. OrgForge is available under the MIT license.

摘要：評估檢索增強生成（RAG）管道需要具有可知的真實情況、時間結構化的語料庫，以及現實世界數據集很少能夠乾淨提供的跨文物特性。現有資源如恩隆語料庫存在法律模糊性、人口統計偏差，且沒有結構化的真實情況。純粹由LLM生成的合成數據解決了法律問題，但引入了一個更微妙的問題：生成模型無法避免在文檔之間產生互相矛盾的事實幻覺。我們提出OrgForge，一個開源的多代理模擬框架，強制執行嚴格的物理-認知邊界：一個確定性的Python引擎維護一個SimEvent真實情況總線；大型語言模型僅生成表面散文，受限於經過驗證的提案。一個演員本地時鐘強制執行所有文物類型的因果時間戳正確性，消除了當時間戳在每個文檔中獨立抽樣時出現的時間線不一致類別。我們形式化了三個圖動態子系統，通過介於中心性、時間邊權衰減和Dijkstra升級路由來進行壓力傳播，這些子系統獨立於任何LLM來治理組織行為。運行可配置的N天模擬，OrgForge生成交錯的Slack線程、JIRA票據、Confluence頁面、Git拉取請求和電子郵件，所有這些都可以追溯到一個共享的、不可變的事件日誌。我們還描述了一個因果鏈追蹤子系統，該子系統為每個事件累積跨文物證據圖，一個混合的互惠排名融合重複檢測器用於識別重複失敗類別，以及一個進出電子郵件引擎，通過帶有概率丟棄模擬的門控因果鏈路由供應商警報、客戶投訴和人力資源通信。OrgForge在MIT許可下提供。

##### **KGS-GCN: Enhancing Sparse Skeleton Sensing via Kinematics-Driven Gaussian Splatting and Probabilistic Topology for Action Recognition**
2603.16943v1 by Yuhan Chen, Yicui Shi, Guofa Li, Liping Zhang, Jie Li, Jiaxin Gao, Wenbo Chu

Skeleton-based action recognition is widely utilized in sensor systems including human-computer interaction and intelligent surveillance. Nevertheless, current sensor devices typically generate sparse skeleton data as discrete coordinates, which inevitably discards fine-grained spatiotemporal details during highly dynamic movements. Moreover, the rigid constraints of predefined physical sensor topologies hinder the modeling of latent long-range dependencies. To overcome these limitations, we propose KGS-GCN, a graph convolutional network that integrates kinematics-driven Gaussian splatting with probabilistic topology. Our framework explicitly addresses the challenges of sensor data sparsity and topological rigidity by transforming discrete joints into continuous generative representations. Firstly, a kinematics-driven Gaussian splatting module is designed to dynamically construct anisotropic covariance matrices using instantaneous joint velocity vectors. This module enhances visual representation by rendering sparse skeleton sequences into multi-view continuous heatmaps rich in spatiotemporal semantics. Secondly, to transcend the limitations of fixed physical connections, a probabilistic topology construction method is proposed. This approach generates an adaptive prior adjacency matrix by quantifying statistical correlations via the Bhattacharyya distance between joint Gaussian distributions. Ultimately, the GCN backbone is adaptively modulated by the rendered visual features via a visual context gating mechanism. Empirical results demonstrate that KGS-GCN significantly enhances the modeling of complex spatiotemporal dynamics. By addressing the inherent limitations of sparse inputs, our framework offers a robust solution for processing low-fidelity sensor data. This approach establishes a practical pathway for improving perceptual reliability in real-world sensing applications.

摘要：骨架基礎的動作識別廣泛應用於包括人機互動和智能監控在內的傳感器系統。<lb/>然而，目前的傳感器設備通常生成稀疏的骨架數據作為離散坐標，這不可避免地在高度動態的運動中丟失細粒度的時空細節。<lb/>此外，預定義的物理傳感器拓撲的剛性約束妨礙了潛在長距離依賴關係的建模。<lb/>為了克服這些限制，我們提出了KGS-GCN，一種將運動學驅動的高斯噴濺與概率拓撲相結合的圖卷積網絡。<lb/>我們的框架明確解決了傳感器數據稀疏性和拓撲剛性的挑戰，通過將離散關節轉換為連續生成表示。<lb/>首先，設計了一個運動學驅動的高斯噴濺模塊，動態構建各向異性的協方差矩陣，使用瞬時關節速度向量。<lb/>該模塊通過將稀疏骨架序列渲染為富含時空語義的多視角連續熱圖來增強視覺表示。<lb/>其次，為了超越固定物理連接的限制，提出了一種概率拓撲構建方法。<lb/>這種方法通過量化關節高斯分佈之間的Bhattacharyya距離來生成自適應的先驗鄰接矩陣。<lb/>最終，GCN主幹通過視覺上下文閘控機制自適應調整渲染的視覺特徵。<lb/>實證結果表明，KGS-GCN顯著增強了複雜時空動態的建模。<lb/>通過解決稀疏輸入的固有限制，我們的框架為處理低保真度的傳感器數據提供了一個穩健的解決方案。<lb/>這種方法為改善現實世界感知應用中的感知可靠性建立了一條實用途徑。

##### **A Hybrid AI and Rule-Based Decision Support System for Disease Diagnosis and Management Using Labs**
2603.14876v1 by Muhammad Hammad Maqsood, Mubashir Sajid, Khubaib Ahmed, Muhammad Usamah Shahid, Muddassar Farooq

This research paper outlines the development and implementation of a novel Clinical Decision Support System (CDSS) that integrates AI predictive modeling with medical knowledge bases. It utilizes the quantifiable information elements in lab results for inferring likely diagnoses a patient might have. Subsequently, suggesting investigations to confirm the likely diagnoses -- an assistive tool for physicians. The system fuses knowledge contained in a rule-base expert system with inferences of data driven predictors based on the features in labs. The data for 593,055 patients was collected from 547 primary care centers across the US to model our decision support system and derive Real-Word Evidence (RWE) to make it relevant for a large demographic of patients. Our Rule-Base comprises clinically validated rules, modeling 59 health conditions that can directly confirm one or more of diseases and assign ICD-10 codes to them. The Likely Diagnosis system uses multi-class classification, covering 37 ICD-10 codes, which are grouped together into 11 categories based on the labs that physicians prescribe to confirm the diagnosis. This research offers a novel system that assists a physician by utilizing medical profile of a patient and routine lab investigations to predict a group of likely diseases and then confirm them, coupled with providing explanations for inferences, thereby assisting physicians to reduce misdiagnosis of patients in clinical decision-making.

摘要：這篇研究論文概述了一個新型臨床決策支持系統（CDSS）的開發和實施，該系統將人工智慧預測建模與醫學知識庫整合在一起。<lb/>它利用實驗室結果中的可量化信息元素來推斷患者可能擁有的診斷。<lb/>隨後，建議進行檢查以確認可能的診斷——這是一種對醫生的輔助工具。<lb/>該系統融合了基於規則的專家系統中的知識與基於實驗室特徵的數據驅動預測器的推斷。<lb/>我們從美國547個初級保健中心收集了593,055名患者的數據，以建模我們的決策支持系統並推導出實證證據（RWE），使其對大量患者的相關性增強。<lb/>我們的基於規則的系統包含臨床驗證的規則，建模59種健康狀況，這些狀況可以直接確認一種或多種疾病並為其分配ICD-10代碼。<lb/>可能診斷系統使用多類別分類，涵蓋37個ICD-10代碼，這些代碼根據醫生開立的實驗室檢查以確認診斷而分為11類。<lb/>這項研究提供了一個新系統，通過利用患者的醫療檔案和常規實驗室檢查來預測一組可能的疾病，然後確認這些疾病，並提供推斷的解釋，從而幫助醫生減少臨床決策中的誤診。

##### **Sample-Efficient Hypergradient Estimation for Decentralized Bi-Level Reinforcement Learning**
2603.14867v1 by Mikoto Kudo, Takumi Tanabe, Akifumi Wachi, Youhei Akimoto

Many strategic decision-making problems, such as environment design for warehouse robots, can be naturally formulated as bi-level reinforcement learning (RL), where a leader agent optimizes its objective while a follower solves a Markov decision process (MDP) conditioned on the leader's decisions. In many situations, a fundamental challenge arises when the leader cannot intervene in the follower's optimization process; it can only observe the optimization outcome. We address this decentralized setting by deriving the hypergradient of the leader's objective, i.e., the gradient of the leader's strategy that accounts for changes in the follower's optimal policy. Unlike prior hypergradient-based methods that require extensive data for repeated state visits or rely on gradient estimators whose complexity can increase substantially with the high-dimensional leader's decision space, we leverage the Boltzmann covariance trick to derive an alternative hypergradient formulation. This enables efficient hypergradient estimation solely from interaction samples, even when the leader's decision space is high-dimensional. Additionally, to our knowledge, this is the first method that enables hypergradient-based optimization for 2-player Markov games in decentralized settings. Experiments highlight the impact of hypergradient updates and demonstrate our method's effectiveness in both discrete and continuous state tasks.

摘要：許多戰略決策問題，例如倉庫機器人的環境設計，可以自然地表述為雙層增強學習（RL），其中領導代理優化其目標，而跟隨者根據領導者的決策解決馬爾可夫決策過程（MDP）。在許多情況下，當領導者無法介入跟隨者的優化過程時，會出現一個基本挑戰；它只能觀察優化結果。我們通過推導領導者目標的超梯度來解決這種去中心化的設置，即考慮到跟隨者最優策略變化的領導者策略的梯度。與以往需要大量數據以進行重複狀態訪問的基於超梯度的方法或依賴於隨著高維領導者決策空間而顯著增加複雜性的梯度估計器的方法不同，我們利用玻爾茲曼協方差技巧推導出一種替代的超梯度表述。這使得即使在領導者的決策空間是高維的情況下，也能僅通過互動樣本有效地估計超梯度。此外，據我們所知，這是第一種能夠在去中心化設置中實現基於超梯度的優化的2人馬爾可夫遊戲的方法。實驗突顯了超梯度更新的影響，並展示了我們的方法在離散和連續狀態任務中的有效性。

##### **The Impact of Ideological Discourses in RAG: A Case Study with COVID-19 Treatments**
2603.14838v1 by Elmira Salari, Maria Claudia Nunes Delfino, Hazem Amamou, José Victor de Souza, Shruti Kshirsagar, Alan Davoust, Anderson Avila

This paper studies the impact of retrieved ideological texts on the outputs of large language models (LLMs). While interest in understanding ideology in LLMs has recently increased, little attention has been given to this issue in the context of Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG). To fill this gap, we design an external knowledge source based on ideological loaded texts about COVID-19 treatments. Our corpus is based on 1,117 academic articles representing discourses about controversial and endorsed treatments for the disease. We propose a corpus linguistics framework, based on Lexical Multidimensional Analysis (LMDA), to identify the ideologies within the corpus. LLMs are tasked to answer questions derived from three identified ideological dimensions, and two types of contextual prompts are adopted: the first comprises the user question and ideological texts; and the second contains the question, ideological texts, and LMDA descriptions. Ideological alignment between reference ideological texts and LLMs' responses is assessed using cosine similarity for lexical and semantic representations. Results demonstrate that LLMs' responses based on ideological retrieved texts are more aligned with the ideology encountered in the external knowledge, with the enhanced prompt further influencing LLMs' outputs. Our findings highlight the importance of identifying ideological discourses within the RAG framework in order to mitigate not just unintended ideological bias, but also the risks of malicious manipulation of such models.

摘要：這篇論文研究了檢索到的意識形態文本對大型語言模型（LLMs）輸出的影響。雖然最近對理解LLMs中的意識形態的興趣有所增加，但在檢索增強生成（RAG）的背景下，對此問題的關注卻很少。為了填補這一空白，我們設計了一個基於有關COVID-19治療的意識形態文本的外部知識來源。我們的語料庫基於1,117篇學術文章，代表了有關該疾病的爭議性和被認可的治療的論述。我們提出了一個基於詞彙多維分析（LMDA）的語料語言學框架，以識別語料庫中的意識形態。LLMs的任務是回答來自三個已識別意識形態維度的問題，並採用兩種類型的上下文提示：第一種包括用戶問題和意識形態文本；第二種包含問題、意識形態文本和LMDA描述。通過餘弦相似度來評估參考意識形態文本與LLMs回應之間的意識形態一致性，針對詞彙和語義表徵。結果表明，基於檢索到的意識形態文本的LLMs回應與外部知識中遇到的意識形態更為一致，增強的提示進一步影響了LLMs的輸出。我們的研究結果突顯了在RAG框架內識別意識形態論述的重要性，以減少不僅是無意的意識形態偏見，還有這些模型惡意操縱的風險。

##### **Planning as Goal Recognition: Deriving Heuristics from Intention Models - Extended Version**
2603.14824v1 by Giacomo Rosa, Jean Honorio, Nir Lipovetzky, Sebastian Sardina

Classical planning aims to find a sequence of actions, a plan, that maps a starting state into one of the goal states. If a trajectory appears to be leading to the goal, should we prioritise exploring it? Seminal work in goal recognition (GR) has defined GR in terms of a classical planning problem, adopting classical solvers and heuristics to recognise plans. We come full circle, and study the adoption and properties of GR-derived heuristics for seeking solutions to classical planning problems. We propose a new framework for assessing goal intention, which informs a new class of efficiently-computable heuristics. As a proof of concept, we derive two such heuristics, and show that they can already yield improvements for top-scoring classical planners. Our work provides foundational knowledge for understanding and deriving probabilistic intention-based heuristics for planning.

摘要：古典規劃旨在找到一系列行動，即計劃，將起始狀態映射到目標狀態之一。<lb/>如果一條軌跡似乎正在通向目標，我們應該優先探索它嗎？<lb/>在目標識別（GR）方面的開創性工作已將GR定義為一個古典規劃問題，採用古典求解器和啟發式方法來識別計劃。<lb/>我們回到起點，研究GR衍生的啟發式方法在尋求古典規劃問題解決方案中的採用和特性。<lb/>我們提出了一個新的框架來評估目標意圖，這為一類高效可計算的啟發式方法提供了依據。<lb/>作為概念驗證，我們推導出兩種此類啟發式方法，並顯示它們已經能為得分最高的古典規劃者帶來改進。<lb/>我們的工作為理解和推導基於概率的意圖啟發式方法在規劃中的應用提供了基礎知識。

##### **RAZOR: Ratio-Aware Layer Editing for Targeted Unlearning in Vision Transformers and Diffusion Models**
2603.14819v1 by Ravi Ranjan, Utkarsh Grover, Xiaomin Lin, Agoritsa Polyzou

Transformer based diffusion and vision-language models have achieved remarkable success; yet, efficiently removing undesirable or sensitive information without retraining remains a central challenge for model safety and compliance. We introduce Ratio-Aware Zero/One-step Optimized Retentive unlearning (RAZOR), a lightweight, model-agnostic unlearning framework that generalizes forgetting updates to coordinated multi-layer and multi-head edits within transformer backbones. RAZOR identifies the most important layers and attention heads by measuring how much they contribute to forgetting the target data while preserving useful knowledge. Then, it updates these parts of the model using a carefully regularized rule to avoid harming overall performance. The set of edited components grows gradually, ensuring precise unlearning without over-editing or damaging unrelated capabilities. We evaluate RAZOR on CLIP, Stable Diffusion, and vision-language models (VLMs) using widely adopted unlearning benchmarks covering identity, style, and object erasure tasks. Our results show that RAZOR achieves highly accurate and stable forgetting, even under quantization. This approach offers stronger retention and better efficiency than prior methods. Notably, it also operates significant faster than conventional techniques. These results demonstrate that RAZOR is a practical and scalable solution for safe, adaptive unlearning in transformer-based vision models.

摘要：Transformer基礎的擴散和視覺-語言模型已取得顯著成功；然而，在不重新訓練的情況下有效地移除不必要或敏感的信息仍然是模型安全性和合規性的一個核心挑戰。我們介紹了比例感知的零/一步優化保持性遺忘（RAZOR），這是一個輕量級、模型無關的遺忘框架，將遺忘更新概括為Transformer骨幹內的協調多層和多頭編輯。RAZOR通過測量最重要的層和注意力頭對於遺忘目標數據的貢獻程度來識別它們，同時保留有用的知識。然後，它使用經過仔細正則化的規則更新模型的這些部分，以避免損害整體性能。編輯組件的集合逐漸增長，確保精確的遺忘，而不會過度編輯或損害不相關的能力。我們在CLIP、穩定擴散和視覺-語言模型（VLMs）上評估RAZOR，使用廣泛採用的遺忘基準，涵蓋身份、風格和物體刪除任務。我們的結果顯示，RAZOR在量化下也能實現高度準確和穩定的遺忘。這種方法提供了比以前的方法更強的保持性和更好的效率。值得注意的是，它的運行速度也顯著快於傳統技術。這些結果表明，RAZOR是一個實用且可擴展的解決方案，適用於基於Transformer的視覺模型中的安全、自適應遺忘。

##### **Knowledge Activation: AI Skills as the Institutional Knowledge Primitive for Agentic Software Development**
2603.14805v1 by Gal Bakal

Enterprise software organizations accumulate critical institutional knowledge - architectural decisions, deployment procedures, compliance policies, incident playbooks - yet this knowledge remains trapped in formats designed for human interpretation. The bottleneck to effective agentic software development is not model capability but knowledge architecture. When any knowledge consumer - an autonomous AI agent, a newly onboarded engineer, or a senior developer - encounters an enterprise task without institutional context, the result is guesswork, correction cascades, and a disproportionate tax on senior engineers who must manually supply what others cannot infer.
  This paper introduces Knowledge Activation, a framework that specializes AI Skills - the open standard for agent-consumable knowledge - into structured, governance-aware Atomic Knowledge Units (AKUs) for institutional knowledge delivery. Rather than retrieving documents for interpretation, AKUs deliver action - ready specifications encoding what to do, which tools to use, what constraints to respect, and where to go next - so that agents act correctly and engineers receive institutionally grounded guidance without reconstructing organizational context from scratch.
  AKUs form a composable knowledge graph that agents traverse at runtime - compressing onboarding, reducing cross - team friction, and eliminating correction cascades. The paper formalizes the resource constraints that make this architecture necessary, specifies the AKU schema and deployment architecture, and grounds long - term maintenance in knowledge commons practice. Organizations that architect their institutional knowledge for the agentic era will outperform those that invest solely in model capability.

摘要：企業軟體組織積累了關鍵的制度知識——架構決策、部署程序、合規政策、事件應對手冊——然而這些知識仍然被困在為人類解讀而設計的格式中。有效的自主軟體開發的瓶頸不是模型能力，而是知識架構。當任何知識消費者——一個自主的AI代理、新上任的工程師或資深開發者——在沒有制度背景的情況下遇到企業任務時，結果就是猜測、修正連鎖反應，以及對資深工程師的不成比例的壓力，他們必須手動提供其他人無法推斷的內容。<lb/>
本文介紹了知識激活（Knowledge Activation），這是一個專門將AI技能（AI Skills）——可供代理使用的知識的開放標準——轉化為結構化、具有治理意識的原子知識單元（Atomic Knowledge Units, AKUs）以便交付制度知識的框架。AKUs不是檢索文件以進行解讀，而是提供行動——準備好的規範，編碼了該做什麼、使用哪些工具、遵循哪些限制以及接下來該去哪裡——使得代理能夠正確行動，工程師能夠在不必從零開始重建組織背景的情況下獲得制度基礎的指導。<lb/>
AKUs形成了一個可組合的知識圖譜，代理在運行時遍歷——壓縮了入職培訓，減少了跨團隊摩擦，並消除了修正連鎖反應。本文正式化了使這種架構成為必要的資源限制，具體說明了AKU架構和部署架構，並將長期維護根植於知識共享的實踐中。那些為自主時代架構其制度知識的組織將超越那些僅僅投資於模型能力的組織。

#### Abstracts
##### **KineVLA: Towards Kinematics-Aware Vision-Language-Action Models with Bi-Level Action Decomposition**
2603.17524v1 by Gaoge Han, Zhengqing Gao, Ziwen Li, Jiaxin Huang, Shaoli Huang, Fakhri Karray, Mingming Gong, Tongliang Liu

In this paper, we introduce a novel kinematics-rich vision-language-action (VLA) task, in which language commands densely encode diverse kinematic attributes (such as direction, trajectory, orientation, and relative displacement) from initiation through completion, at key moments, unlike existing action instructions that capture kinematics only coarsely or partially, thereby supporting fine-grained and personalized manipulation. In this setting, where task goals remain invariant while execution trajectories must adapt to instruction-level kinematic specifications. To address this challenge, we propose KineVLA, a vision-language-action framework that explicitly decouples goal-level invariance from kinematics-level variability through a bi-level action representation and bi-level reasoning tokens to serve as explicit, supervised intermediate variables that align language and action. To support this task, we construct the kinematics-aware VLA datasets spanning both simulation and real-world robotic platforms, featuring instruction-level kinematic variations and bi-level annotations. Extensive experiments on LIBERO and a Realman-75 robot demonstrate that KineVLA consistently outperforms strong VLA baselines on kinematics-sensitive benchmarks, achieving more precise, controllable, and generalizable manipulation behaviors.

摘要：在本文中，我們介紹了一個新穎的運動學豐富的視覺-語言-行動（VLA）任務，其中語言命令密集編碼了多樣的運動學屬性（例如方向、軌跡、方位和相對位移），從開始到完成，在關鍵時刻，與現有的僅粗略或部分捕捉運動學的行動指令不同，從而支持細緻和個性化的操作。在這種情境中，任務目標保持不變，而執行軌跡必須適應指令級的運動學規範。為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了KineVLA，一個視覺-語言-行動框架，通過雙層行動表示和雙層推理標記明確地將目標級不變性與運動學級變異性解耦，以作為明確的、有監督的中介變量，對齊語言和行動。為了支持這項任務，我們構建了運動學感知的VLA數據集，涵蓋了模擬和現實世界的機器人平台，具有指令級的運動學變異和雙層標註。在LIBERO和Realman-75機器人上的廣泛實驗表明，KineVLA在運動學敏感的基準上始終優於強大的VLA基線，實現了更精確、可控和可泛化的操作行為。

##### **Detecting the Machine: A Comprehensive Benchmark of AI-Generated Text Detectors Across Architectures, Domains, and Adversarial Conditions**
2603.17522v1 by Madhav S. Baidya, S. S. Baidya, Chirag Chawla

The rapid proliferation of large language models (LLMs) has created an urgent need for robust and generalizable detectors of machine-generated text. Existing benchmarks typically evaluate a single detector on a single dataset under ideal conditions, leaving open questions about cross-domain transfer, cross-LLM generalization, and adversarial robustness.
  We present a comprehensive benchmark evaluating diverse detection approaches across two corpora: HC3 (23,363 human-ChatGPT pairs) and ELI5 (15,000 human-Mistral-7B pairs). Methods include classical classifiers, fine-tuned transformer encoders (BERT, RoBERTa, ELECTRA, DistilBERT, DeBERTa-v3), a CNN, an XGBoost stylometric model, perplexity-based detectors, and LLM-as-detector prompting.
  Results show that transformer models achieve near-perfect in-distribution performance but degrade under domain shift. The XGBoost stylometric model matches performance while remaining interpretable. LLM-based detectors underperform and are affected by generator-detector identity bias. Perplexity-based methods exhibit polarity inversion, with modern LLM outputs showing lower perplexity than human text, but remain effective when corrected. No method generalizes robustly across domains and LLM sources.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）的快速增長使得對於機器生成文本的穩健且可泛化的檢測器產生了迫切需求。現有的基準通常在理想條件下評估單一檢測器在單一數據集上的表現，這留下了關於跨領域轉移、跨LLM泛化和對抗穩健性的未解問題。<lb/>  
我們提出了一個綜合基準，評估兩個語料庫中多樣的檢測方法：HC3（23,363對人類-ChatGPT）和ELI5（15,000對人類-Mistral-7B）。方法包括傳統分類器、微調的Transformer編碼器（BERT、RoBERTa、ELECTRA、DistilBERT、DeBERTa-v3）、CNN、一個XGBoost風格模型、基於困惑度的檢測器，以及LLM作為檢測器的提示。<lb/>  
結果顯示，Transformer模型在分佈內的表現接近完美，但在領域轉移時表現下降。XGBoost風格模型在保持可解釋性的同時匹配了性能。基於LLM的檢測器表現不佳，並受到生成器-檢測器身份偏見的影響。基於困惑度的方法顯示出極性反轉，現代LLM的輸出顯示出比人類文本更低的困惑度，但在修正後仍然有效。沒有任何方法能在不同領域和LLM來源之間穩健地泛化。

##### **Language on Demand, Knowledge at Core: Composing LLMs with Encoder-Decoder Translation Models for Extensible Multilinguality**
2603.17512v1 by Mengyu Bu, Yang Feng

Large language models (LLMs) exhibit strong general intelligence, yet their multilingual performance remains highly imbalanced. Although LLMs encode substantial cross-lingual knowledge in a unified semantic space, they often struggle to reliably interface this knowledge with low-resource or unseen languages. Fortunately, pretrained encoder-decoder translation models already possess balanced multilingual capability, suggesting a natural complement to LLMs. In this work, we propose XBridge, a compositional encoder-LLM-decoder architecture that offloads multilingual understanding and generation to external pretrained translation models, while preserving the LLM as an English-centric core for general knowledge processing. To address the resulting representation misalignment across models, we introduce lightweight cross-model mapping layers and an optimal transport-based alignment objective, enabling fine-grained semantic consistency for multilingual generation. Experiments on four LLMs across multilingual understanding, reasoning, summarization, and generation indicate that XBridge outperforms strong baselines, especially on low-resource and previously unseen languages, without retraining the LLM.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）展現出強大的通用智慧，但它們的多語言表現仍然高度不平衡。儘管LLMs在統一的語義空間中編碼了大量的跨語言知識，但它們在與低資源或未見語言可靠地對接這些知識時經常遇到困難。幸運的是，預訓練的編碼器-解碼器翻譯模型已經具備平衡的多語言能力，這表明它們可以自然地補充LLMs。在本研究中，我們提出了XBridge，一種組合的編碼器-LLM-解碼器架構，將多語言理解和生成的任務轉移到外部預訓練的翻譯模型，同時保留LLM作為以英語為中心的核心，用於一般知識處理。為了解決模型之間的表示不對齊問題，我們引入了輕量級的跨模型映射層和基於最佳運輸的對齊目標，從而實現多語言生成的細粒度語義一致性。在四個LLMs上進行的多語言理解、推理、總結和生成的實驗表明，XBridge在強基準之上表現出色，特別是在低資源和之前未見的語言上，且無需重新訓練LLM。

##### **QuantFL: Sustainable Federated Learning for Edge IoT via Pre-Trained Model Quantisation**
2603.17507v1 by Charuka Herath, Yogachandran Rahulamathavan, Varuna De Silva, Sangarapillai Lambotharan

Federated Learning (FL) enables privacy-preserving intelligence on Internet of Things (IoT) devices but incurs a significant carbon footprint due to the high energy cost of frequent uplink transmission. While pre-trained models are increasingly available on edge devices, their potential to reduce the energy overhead of fine-tuning remains underexplored. In this work, we propose QuantFL, a sustainable FL framework that leverages pre-trained initialisation to enable aggressive, computationally lightweight quantisation. We demonstrate that pre-training naturally concentrates update statistics, allowing us to use memory-efficient bucket quantisation without the energy-intensive overhead of complex error-feedback mechanisms. On MNIST and CIFAR-100, QuantFL reduces total communication by 40\% ($\simeq40\%$ total-bit reduction with full-precision downlink; $\geq80\%$ on uplink or when downlink is quantised) while matching or exceeding uncompressed baselines under strict bandwidth budgets; BU attains 89.00\% (MNIST) and 66.89\% (CIFAR-100) test accuracy with orders of magnitude fewer bits. We also account for uplink and downlink costs and provide ablations on quantisation levels and initialisation. QuantFL delivers a practical, "green" recipe for scalable training on battery-constrained IoT networks.

摘要：聯邦學習（FL）在物聯網（IoT）設備上實現了保護隱私的智能，但由於頻繁上行傳輸的高能耗，造成了顯著的碳足跡。儘管邊緣設備上越來越多可用的預訓練模型，但它們在減少微調的能源開銷方面的潛力仍未被充分探索。在這項工作中，我們提出了QuantFL，一個可持續的FL框架，利用預訓練初始化來實現激進的、計算輕量的量化。我們展示了預訓練自然集中更新統計，使我們能夠使用內存高效的桶量化，而無需複雜的錯誤反饋機制所需的高能耗開銷。在MNIST和CIFAR-100上，QuantFL將總通信量減少了40\%（$\simeq40\%$的全精度下行位元減少；上行或下行量化時則$\geq80\%$），同時在嚴格的帶寬預算下達到或超過未壓縮基準；BU在僅使用數量級更少的位元的情況下，實現了89.00\%（MNIST）和66.89\%（CIFAR-100）的測試準確率。我們還考慮了上行和下行的成本，並提供了對量化水平和初始化的消融實驗。QuantFL為在電池受限的IoT網絡上可擴展訓練提供了一個實用的“綠色”方案。

##### **Inducing Epistemological Humility in Large Language Models: A Targeted SFT Approach to Reducing Hallucination**
2603.17504v1 by Cem Uluoglakci, Tugba Taskaya Temizel

Large language models (LLMs) often hallucinate, producing fluent but false information, partly because supervised fine-tuning (SFT) implicitly rewards always responding. We introduce $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$, an SFT dataset (31,487 responses for 11,151 questions) designed to teach models epistemological humility-the ability to recognize the limits of their own knowledge and admit uncertainty. This is achieved through questions about non-existent "hypothetical" terms. We also release $\textit{HypoTermQA-Enhanced}$, a benchmark for hallucination tendency strengthened through multiple validations. We conducted 800 controlled LoRA SFT runs across $\textit{Llama3.1-8B}$ and $\textit{Gemma3-4B}$ (base and instruct), testing 100 fine-tuning configurations with paired controls. Our results demonstrate that replacing generic instruction data with $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$ significantly improves the HypoTerm Score (median increases of 0.19% to 25.91%) and FactScore (+0.39% to +0.86%), while maintaining stable performance on MMLU (minimal decreases of 0.26% to 0.35%). Our work demonstrates that targeted, high-quality SFT data teaching meta-cognitive skills can effectively reduce hallucination without preference/RL pipelines, providing mechanistic insights and a practical path toward more reliable AI systems.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）經常會出現幻覺，產生流暢但虛假的資訊，部分原因是監督式微調（SFT）隱含地獎勵總是回應。我們介紹了 $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$，這是一個 SFT 數據集（31,487 個回應對應 11,151 個問題），旨在教導模型認識認識論的謙遜——識別自身知識的局限性並承認不確定性。這是通過關於不存在的「假設」術語的問題來實現的。我們還發布了 $\textit{HypoTermQA-Enhanced}$，這是一個通過多次驗證強化的幻覺傾向基準。我們在 $\textit{Llama3.1-8B}$ 和 $\textit{Gemma3-4B}$（基礎和指令）上進行了 800 次控制的 LoRA SFT 執行，測試了 100 種微調配置及其配對控制。我們的結果顯示，用 $\textit{HypoTermInstruct}$ 替換通用指令數據顯著提高了 HypoTerm 分數（中位數增加 0.19% 到 25.91%）和 FactScore（+0.39% 到 +0.86%），同時在 MMLU 上保持穩定的表現（最小下降 0.26% 到 0.35%）。我們的工作表明，針對性的高質量 SFT 數據教導元認知技能可以有效減少幻覺，而無需偏好/RL 管道，提供了機制上的見解和通向更可靠 AI 系統的實用途徑。

##### **Learning When to Attend: Conditional Memory Access for Long-Context LLMs**
2603.17484v1 by Sakshi Choudhary, Aditya Chattopadhyay, Luca Zancato, Elvis Nunez, Matthew Trager, Wei Xia, Stefano Soatto

Language models struggle to generalize beyond pretraining context lengths, limiting long-horizon reasoning and retrieval. Continued pretraining on long-context data can help but is expensive due to the quadratic scaling of Attention. We observe that most tokens do not require (Global) Attention over the entire sequence and can rely on local context. Based on this, we propose L2A (Learning To Attend), a layer that enables conditional (token-wise) long-range memory access by deciding when to invoke global attention. We evaluate L2A on Qwen 2.5 and Qwen 3 models, extending their effective context length from 32K to 128K tokens. L2A matches the performance of standard long-context training to within 3% while skipping Global Attention for $\sim$80% of tokens, outperforming prior baselines. We also design custom Triton kernels to efficiently implement this token-wise conditional Attention on GPUs, achieving up to $\sim$2x improvements in training throughput and time-to-first-token over FlashAttention. Moreover, L2A enables post-training pruning of highly sparse Global Attention layers, reducing KV cache memory by up to 50% with negligible performance loss.

摘要：語言模型在預訓練上下文長度之外的泛化能力有限，這限制了長期推理和檢索。對長上下文數據的持續預訓練可以有所幫助，但由於注意力的二次擴展，這是昂貴的。我們觀察到大多數標記不需要在整個序列上使用（全局）注意力，並且可以依賴局部上下文。基於此，我們提出了 L2A（學習注意），這是一個層，通過決定何時調用全局注意來實現條件（標記級別）長期記憶訪問。我們在 Qwen 2.5 和 Qwen 3 模型上評估 L2A，將其有效上下文長度從 32K 擴展到 128K 標記。L2A 的性能與標準長上下文訓練相當，誤差在 3% 以內，同時對約 80% 的標記跳過全局注意，超越了之前的基準。我們還設計了自定義 Triton 核心，以高效地在 GPU 上實現這種標記級別的條件注意，實現了訓練吞吐量和首次標記時間的約 2 倍提升，超過了 FlashAttention。此外，L2A 使得對高度稀疏的全局注意層進行後訓練修剪成為可能，將 KV 緩存內存減少了最多 50%，且性能損失微乎其微。

##### **Auto-Unrolled Proximal Gradient Descent: An AutoML Approach to Interpretable Waveform Optimization**
2603.17478v1 by Ahmet Kaplan

This study explores the combination of automated machine learning (AutoML) with model-based deep unfolding (DU) for optimizing wireless beamforming and waveforms. We convert the iterative proximal gradient descent (PGD) algorithm into a deep neural network, wherein the parameters of each layer are learned instead of being predetermined. Additionally, we enhance the architecture by incorporating a hybrid layer that performs a learnable linear gradient transformation prior to the proximal projection. By utilizing AutoGluon with a tree-structured parzen estimator (TPE) for hyperparameter optimization (HPO) across an expanded search space, which includes network depth, step-size initialization, optimizer, learning rate scheduler, layer type, and post-gradient activation, the proposed auto-unrolled PGD (Auto-PGD) achieves 98.8% of the spectral efficiency of a traditional 200-iteration PGD solver using only five unrolled layers, while requiring only 100 training samples. We also address a gradient normalization issue to ensure consistent performance during training and evaluation, and we illustrate per-layer sum-rate logging as a tool for transparency. These contributions highlight a notable reduction in the amount of training data and inference cost required, while maintaining high interpretability compared to conventional black-box architectures.

摘要：這項研究探討自動化機器學習（AutoML）與基於模型的深度展開（DU）結合，以優化無線波束形成和波形。我們將迭代的近端梯度下降（PGD）算法轉換為深度神經網絡，其中每一層的參數是學習得到的，而不是預先設定的。此外，我們通過引入一個混合層來增強架構，該層在近端投影之前執行可學習的線性梯度變換。通過利用 AutoGluon 和樹狀 Parzen 估計器（TPE）進行超參數優化（HPO），在擴展的搜索空間中，包括網絡深度、步長初始化、優化器、學習率調度器、層類型和後梯度激活，所提出的自動展開 PGD（Auto-PGD）在僅使用五個展開層的情況下，達到了傳統 200 次迭代 PGD 求解器 98.8% 的光譜效率，同時僅需 100 個訓練樣本。我們還解決了梯度正規化問題，以確保在訓練和評估過程中的一致性能，並展示每層的總速率日誌作為透明度的工具。這些貢獻突顯了所需訓練數據和推理成本的顯著減少，同時與傳統的黑箱架構相比，保持了高可解釋性。

##### **UniSAFE: A Comprehensive Benchmark for Safety Evaluation of Unified Multimodal Models**
2603.17476v1 by Segyu Lee, Boryeong Cho, Hojung Jung, Seokhyun An, Juhyeong Kim, Jaehyun Kwak, Yongjin Yang, Sangwon Jang, Youngrok Park, Wonjun Chang, Se-Young Yun

Unified Multimodal Models (UMMs) offer powerful cross-modality capabilities but introduce new safety risks not observed in single-task models. Despite their emergence, existing safety benchmarks remain fragmented across tasks and modalities, limiting the comprehensive evaluation of complex system-level vulnerabilities. To address this gap, we introduce UniSAFE, the first comprehensive benchmark for system-level safety evaluation of UMMs across 7 I/O modality combinations, spanning conventional tasks and novel multimodal-context image generation settings. UniSAFE is built with a shared-target design that projects common risk scenarios across task-specific I/O configurations, enabling controlled cross-task comparisons of safety failures. Comprising 6,802 curated instances, we use UniSAFE to evaluate 15 state-of-the-art UMMs, both proprietary and open-source. Our results reveal critical vulnerabilities across current UMMs, including elevated safety violations in multi-image composition and multi-turn settings, with image-output tasks consistently more vulnerable than text-output tasks. These findings highlight the need for stronger system-level safety alignment for UMMs. Our code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/segyulee/UniSAFE

摘要：統一多模態模型（UMMs）提供強大的跨模態能力，但引入了在單一任務模型中未觀察到的新安全風險。儘管它們已經出現，現有的安全基準在任務和模態上仍然支離破碎，限制了對複雜系統級脆弱性的全面評估。為了解決這一問題，我們推出了UniSAFE，這是首個針對UMMs在7種I/O模態組合下進行系統級安全評估的綜合基準，涵蓋了傳統任務和新穎的多模態上下文圖像生成設置。UniSAFE採用共享目標設計，能夠在任務特定的I/O配置中投影共同的風險場景，從而實現安全失敗的受控跨任務比較。UniSAFE包含6,802個精心策劃的實例，我們用它來評估15個最先進的UMMs，包括專有和開源模型。我們的結果揭示了當前UMMs的關鍵脆弱性，包括在多圖像組合和多輪設置中安全違規的增加，且圖像輸出任務的脆弱性始終高於文本輸出任務。這些發現突顯了對UMMs進行更強系統級安全對齊的必要性。我們的代碼和數據可在https://github.com/segyulee/UniSAFE公開獲取。

##### **Humans and transformer LMs: Abstraction drives language learning**
2603.17475v1 by Jasper Jian, Christopher D. Manning

Categorization is a core component of human linguistic competence. We investigate how a transformer-based language model (LM) learns linguistic categories by comparing its behaviour over the course of training to behaviours which characterize abstract feature-based and concrete exemplar-based accounts of human language acquisition. We investigate how lexical semantic and syntactic categories emerge using novel divergence-based metrics that track learning trajectories using next-token distributions. In experiments with GPT-2 small, we find that (i) when a construction is learned, abstract class-level behaviour is evident at earlier steps than lexical item-specific behaviour, and (ii) that different linguistic behaviours emerge abruptly in sequence at different points in training, revealing that abstraction plays a key role in how LMs learn. This result informs the models of human language acquisition that LMs may serve as an existence proof for.
