##### **REAL: Regression-Aware Reinforcement Learning for LLM-as-a-Judge**
2603.17145v1 by Yasi Zhang, Tianyu Chen, Mingyuan Zhou, Oscar Leong, Ying Nian Wu, Michal Lukasik

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as automated evaluators that assign numeric scores to model outputs, a paradigm known as LLM-as-a-Judge. However, standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) methods typically rely on binary rewards (e.g., 0-1 accuracy), thereby ignoring the ordinal structure inherent in regression tasks; for instance, they fail to recognize that predicting 4 is significantly better than predicting 1 when the ground truth is 5. Conversely, existing regression-aware approaches are often confined to Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), limiting their ability to explore optimal reasoning paths. To bridge this gap, we propose \textbf{REAL} (\underline{RE}gression-\underline{A}ware Reinforcement \underline{L}earning), a principled RL framework designed to optimize regression rewards, and also proven to be optimal for correlation metrics. A key technical challenge is that the regression objective is explicitly policy-dependent, thus invalidating standard policy gradient methods. To address this, we employ the generalized policy gradient estimator, which naturally decomposes optimization into two complementary components: (1) exploration over Chain-of-Thought (CoT) trajectory, and (2) regression-aware prediction refinement of the final score. Extensive experiments across model scales (8B to 32B) demonstrate that REAL consistently outperforms both regression-aware SFT baselines and standard RL methods, exhibiting significantly better generalization on out-of-domain benchmarks. On Qwen3-32B specifically, we achieve gains of +8.40 Pearson and +7.20 Spearman correlation over the SFT baseline, and +18.30/+11.20 over the base model. These findings highlight the critical value of integrating regression objectives into RL exploration for accurate LLM evaluation.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用作自動評估者，為模型輸出分配數字分數，這一範式被稱為LLM-as-a-Judge。<lb/>然而，標準的強化學習（RL）方法通常依賴於二元獎勵（例如，0-1準確率），因此忽略了回歸任務中固有的序數結構；例如，它們未能識別出當真實值為5時，預測4明顯優於預測1。<lb/>相反，現有的回歸感知方法通常僅限於監督微調（SFT），限制了它們探索最佳推理路徑的能力。<lb/>為了填補這一空白，我們提出了\textbf{REAL}（\underline{RE}gression-\underline{A}ware Reinforcement \underline{L}earning），這是一個旨在優化回歸獎勵的原則性RL框架，並且已被證明在相關性指標上是最佳的。<lb/>一個關鍵的技術挑戰是回歸目標顯式依賴於策略，從而使標準的策略梯度方法失效。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們採用了廣義策略梯度估計器，這自然將優化分解為兩個互補的組件：（1）在思維鏈（CoT）軌跡上的探索，以及（2）對最終分數的回歸感知預測精煉。<lb/>在不同模型規模（8B到32B）上的廣泛實驗表明，REAL始終優於回歸感知的SFT基準和標準的RL方法，在域外基準上展現出顯著更好的泛化能力。<lb/>具體而言，在Qwen3-32B上，我們在SFT基準上實現了+8.40的Pearson和+7.20的Spearman相關性增益，相較於基礎模型則為+18.30/+11.20。<lb/>這些發現突顯了將回歸目標整合到RL探索中以實現準確LLM評估的關鍵價值。

##### **Security Assessment and Mitigation Strategies for Large Language Models: A Comprehensive Defensive Framework**
2603.17123v1 by Taiwo Onitiju, Iman Vakilinia

Large Language Models increasingly power critical infrastructure from healthcare to finance, yet their vulnerability to adversarial manipulation threatens system integrity and user safety. Despite growing deployment, no comprehensive comparative security assessment exists across major LLM architectures, leaving organizations unable to quantify risk or select appropriately secure LLMs for sensitive applications. This research addresses this gap by establishing a standardized vulnerability assessment framework and developing a multi-layered defensive system to protect against identified threats. We systematically evaluate five widely-deployed LLM families GPT-4, GPT-3.5 Turbo, Claude-3 Haiku, LLaMA-2-70B, and Gemini-2.5-pro against 10,000 adversarial prompts spanning six attack categories. Our assessment reveals critical security disparities, with vulnerability rates ranging from 11.9\% to 29.8\%, demonstrating that LLM capability does not correlate with security robustness. To mitigate these risks, we develop a production-ready defensive framework achieving 83\% average detection accuracy with only 5\% false positives. These results demonstrate that systematic security assessment combined with external defensive measures provides a viable path toward safer LLM deployment in production environments.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地驅動著從醫療到金融的關鍵基礎設施，但它們對對抗性操控的脆弱性威脅著系統的完整性和用戶的安全。儘管部署不斷增加，但目前尚無針對主要LLM架構的全面比較安全評估，這使得組織無法量化風險或為敏感應用選擇適當安全的LLM。本研究通過建立標準化的脆弱性評估框架並開發多層防禦系統來保護免受已識別威脅的影響，來填補這一空白。我們系統地評估了五個廣泛部署的LLM家族：GPT-4、GPT-3.5 Turbo、Claude-3 Haiku、LLaMA-2-70B和Gemini-2.5-pro，針對10,000個涵蓋六種攻擊類別的對抗性提示。我們的評估揭示了關鍵的安全差異，脆弱性率範圍從11.9\%到29.8\%，顯示LLM的能力與安全穩健性之間並無相關性。為了減輕這些風險，我們開發了一個生產就緒的防禦框架，實現了83\%的平均檢測準確率，並且只有5\%的假陽性。這些結果表明，系統性的安全評估結合外部防禦措施為在生產環境中更安全地部署LLM提供了一條可行的途徑。

##### **Cascade-Aware Multi-Agent Routing: Spatio-Temporal Sidecars and Geometry-Switching**
2603.17112v1 by Davide Di Gioia

A common architectural pattern in advanced AI reasoning systems is the symbolic graph network: specialized agents or modules connected by delegation edges, routing tasks through a dynamic execution graph. Current schedulers optimize load and fitness but are geometry-blind: they do not model how failures propagate differently in tree-like versus cyclic regimes. In tree-like delegation, a single failure can cascade exponentially; in dense cyclic graphs, failures tend to self-limit. We identify this observability gap, quantify its system-level cost, and propose a lightweight mitigation.
  We formulate online geometry control for route-risk estimation on time-indexed execution graphs with route-local failure history. Our approach combines (i) a Euclidean spatio-temporal propagation baseline, (ii) a hyperbolic route-risk model with temporal decay (and optional burst excitation), and (iii) a learned geometry selector over structural features. The selector is a compact MLP (9->12->1) using six topology statistics plus three geometry-aware signals: BFS shell-growth slope, cycle-rank norm, and fitted Poincare curvature. On the Genesis 3 benchmark distribution, adaptive switching improves win rate in the hardest non_tree regime from 64-72% (fixed hyperbolic variants) to 92%, and achieves 87.2% overall win rate.
  To measure total system value, we compare against Genesis 3 routing without any spatio-temporal sidecar, using only native bandit/LinUCB signals (team fitness and mean node load). This baseline achieves 50.4% win rate overall and 20% in tree-like regimes; the full sidecar recovers 87.2% overall (+36.8 pp), with +48 to +68 pp gains in tree-like settings, consistent with a cascade-sensitivity analysis. Overall, a 133-parameter sidecar substantially mitigates geometry-blind failure propagation in one high-capability execution-graph system.

摘要：一個在先進 AI 推理系統中常見的架構模式是符號圖網絡：專門的代理或模塊通過委派邊連接，通過動態執行圖路由任務。當前的調度器優化負載和適應性，但對幾何形狀無感：它們未能建模失敗在樹狀與循環範疇中如何以不同方式傳播。在樹狀委派中，單一失敗可能會指數級連鎖；在密集的循環圖中，失敗往往自我限制。我們識別出這一可觀察性差距，量化其系統層面的成本，並提出一種輕量級的緩解方案。<lb/>
我們為基於時間索引的執行圖中的路徑風險估算制定了在線幾何控制，並考慮了路徑本地的失敗歷史。我們的方法結合了 (i) 一個歐幾里得時空傳播基線，(ii) 一個具有時間衰減的雙曲路徑風險模型（及可選的突發激勵），以及 (iii) 一個基於結構特徵的學習幾何選擇器。該選擇器是一個緊湊的 MLP (9-&gt;12-&gt;1)，使用六個拓撲統計數據加上三個幾何感知信號：BFS 外殼增長斜率、循環排名範數和擬合的龐加萊曲率。在 Genesis 3 基準分佈上，自適應切換將最困難的非樹狀範疇的勝率從 64-72%（固定的雙曲變體）提高到 92%，並達到 87.2% 的整體勝率。<lb/>
為了衡量系統的總價值，我們將其與 Genesis 3 路由進行比較，該路由未使用任何時空附加組件，只使用本地的 bandit/LinUCB 信號（團隊適應性和平均節點負載）。這一基線的整體勝率為 50.4%，在樹狀範疇中為 20%；完整的附加組件恢復了 87.2% 的整體勝率（+36.8 個百分點），在樹狀環境中增長了 +48 到 +68 個百分點，與級聯敏感性分析一致。總體而言，一個擁有 133 個參數的附加組件在一個高能力的執行圖系統中顯著減輕了幾何盲失敗傳播的問題。

##### **Hidden Clones: Exposing and Fixing Family Bias in Vision-Language Model Ensembles**
2603.17111v1 by Zacharie Bugaud

Ensembling Vision-Language Models (VLMs) from different providers maximizes benchmark accuracy, yet models from the same architectural family share correlated errors that standard voting ignores. We study this structure across 17 VLMs from 8 families on VQAv2, TextVQA, and GQA. Family-correlated errors reduce effective ensemble dimensionality to 2.5-3.6 independent voters and create a Misleading tier (1.5-6.5% of questions) where correlated majority errors destroy accuracy to 0% despite the best model being correct.
  We propose three family-aware methods. Hierarchical Family Voting (HFV) aggregates within families before voting across them, recovering +18-26 pp on the Misleading tier. QualRCCV, a training-free method weighting models by calibration, family quality, and inverse family size, is the first to beat calibrated voting on all three benchmarks (p<0.05). Learned Candidate Scoring (LCS) trains a cross-validated classifier to re-rank candidate answers using support breadth, family diversity, and model quality, achieving the largest gains: +0.68% VQAv2, +0.61% TextVQA, +2.45% GQA -- all significant -- and is the only learned method that never degrades any benchmark. On VQAv2 test-standard (EvalAI), LCS reaches 87.83% with 12 models, confirming generalization.

摘要：整合來自不同供應商的視覺-語言模型 (VLMs) 可以最大化基準準確率，然而來自同一架構家族的模型共享相關錯誤，這些錯誤在標準投票中被忽略。我們在 VQAv2、TextVQA 和 GQA 上研究了來自 8 個家族的 17 個 VLM 的這一結構。家族相關錯誤將有效的集成維度降低到 2.5-3.6 個獨立投票者，並創造了一個誤導性層級 (1.5-6.5% 的問題)，在這裡相關的多數錯誤將準確度摧毀至 0%，儘管最佳模型是正確的。  
我們提出了三種考慮家族的方法。層級家族投票 (HFV) 在家族內部進行聚合，然後在家族之間投票，恢復了誤導性層級的 +18-26 個百分點。QualRCCV，一種無需訓練的方法，通過校準、家族質量和反向家族大小對模型進行加權，是第一個在所有三個基準上超越校準投票的方法 (p&lt;0.05)。學習候選得分 (LCS) 訓練了一個交叉驗證的分類器，使用支持廣度、家族多樣性和模型質量對候選答案進行重新排序，實現了最大的增益：+0.68% VQAv2、+0.61% TextVQA、+2.45% GQA -- 所有增益均顯著 -- 並且是唯一一個從未降低任何基準的學習方法。在 VQAv2 測試標準 (EvalAI) 上，LCS 以 12 個模型達到 87.83%，確認了泛化能力。

##### **Knowledge Localization in Mixture-of-Experts LLMs Using Cross-Lingual Inconsistency**
2603.17102v1 by Lucas Bandarkar, Alan Ansell, Trevor Cohn

Modern LLMs continue to exhibit significant variance in behavior across languages, such as being able to recall factual information in some languages but not others. While typically studied as a problem to be mitigated, in this work, we propose leveraging this cross-lingual inconsistency as a tool for interpretability in mixture-of-experts (MoE) LLMs. Our knowledge localization framework contrasts routing for sets of languages where the model correctly recalls information from languages where it fails. This allows us to isolate model components that play a functional role in answering about a piece of knowledge. Our method proceeds in two stages: (1) querying the model with difficult factual questions across a diverse set of languages to generate "success" and "failure" activation buckets and then (2) applying a statistical contrastive analysis to the MoE router logits to identify experts important for knowledge. To validate the necessity of this small number of experts for answering a knowledge question, we deactivate them and re-ask the question. We find that despite only deactivating about 20 out of 6000 experts, the model no longer answers correctly in over 40% of cases. Generally, this method provides a realistic and scalable knowledge localization approach to address increasingly complex LLMs.

摘要：現代的LLM在不同語言之間的行為仍然顯示出顯著的變異性，例如能夠在某些語言中回憶事實信息，而在其他語言中則無法。雖然通常將其視為需要減輕的問題，但在本研究中，我們提議利用這種跨語言的不一致性作為解釋混合專家（MoE）LLM的工具。我們的知識定位框架對比了在模型能夠正確回憶信息的語言集與其失敗的語言集的路由。這使我們能夠孤立出在回答某個知識時發揮功能的模型組件。我們的方法分為兩個階段：（1）在多樣的語言集中對模型提出困難的事實問題，以生成“成功”和“失敗”的激活桶，然後（2）對MoE路由器的logits應用統計對比分析，以識別對知識重要的專家。為了驗證這少數專家對回答知識問題的必要性，我們將其停用並重新提出問題。我們發現，儘管僅停用了約20個專家中的6000個，但模型在超過40%的情況下不再正確回答。總的來說，這種方法提供了一種現實且可擴展的知識定位方法，以應對日益複雜的LLM。

##### **Evaluating LLM-Simulated Conversations in Modeling Inconsistent and Uncollaborative Behaviors in Human Social Interaction**
2603.17094v1 by Ryo Kamoi, Ameya Godbole, Longqi Yang, Rui Zhang, Mengting Wan, Pei Zhou

Simulating human conversations using large language models (LLMs) has emerged as a scalable methodology for modeling human social interaction. However, simulating human conversations is challenging because they inherently involve inconsistent and uncollaborative behaviors, such as misunderstandings and interruptions. Analysis comparing inconsistent and uncollaborative behaviors in human- and LLM-generated conversations remains limited, although reproducing these behaviors is integral to simulating human-like and complex social interaction. In this work, we introduce CoCoEval, an evaluation framework that analyzes LLM-simulated conversations by detecting 10 types of inconsistent and uncollaborative behaviors at the turn level using an LLM-as-a-Judge. Using CoCoEval, we evaluate GPT-4.1, GPT-5.1, and Claude Opus 4 by comparing the frequencies of detected behaviors in conversations simulated by each model and in human conversations across academic, business, and governmental meetings, as well as debates. Our analysis shows that (1) under vanilla prompting, LLM-simulated conversations exhibit far fewer inconsistent and uncollaborative behaviors than human conversations; (2) prompt engineering does not provide reliable control over these behaviors, as our results show that different prompts lead to their under- or overproduction; and (3) supervised fine-tuning on human conversations can lead LLMs to overproduce a narrow set of behaviors, such as repetition. Our findings highlight the difficulty of simulating human conversations, raising concerns about the use of LLMs as a proxy for human social interaction.

摘要：模擬人類對話的過程中，使用大型語言模型（LLMs）已成為一種可擴展的方法來模擬人類社交互動。<lb/>然而，模擬人類對話是具有挑戰性的，因為這些對話本質上涉及不一致和不合作的行為，例如誤解和打斷。<lb/>對人類和LLM生成的對話中不一致和不合作行為的比較分析仍然有限，儘管重現這些行為對於模擬類人且複雜的社交互動至關重要。<lb/>在本研究中，我們介紹了CoCoEval，一個評估框架，通過使用LLM作為評判者來檢測10種不一致和不合作行為，分析LLM模擬的對話，並在回合層面進行分析。<lb/>使用CoCoEval，我們評估了GPT-4.1、GPT-5.1和Claude Opus 4，通過比較每個模型模擬的對話中檢測到的行為頻率以及人類在學術、商業和政府會議以及辯論中的對話。<lb/>我們的分析顯示：(1) 在普通提示下，LLM模擬的對話表現出比人類對話少得多的不一致和不合作行為；<lb/>(2) 提示工程並未提供對這些行為的可靠控制，我們的結果顯示不同的提示會導致這些行為的不足或過度產生；<lb/>(3) 在人類對話上進行的監督微調可能會導致LLM過度產生一組狹窄的行為，例如重複。<lb/>我們的發現突顯了模擬人類對話的困難，並引發了對使用LLM作為人類社交互動代理的擔憂。

##### **Ensemble Self-Training for Unsupervised Machine Translation**
2603.17087v1 by Ido Aharon, Jonathan Shaki, Sarit Kraus

We present an ensemble-driven self-training framework for unsupervised neural machine translation (UNMT). Starting from a primary language pair, we train multiple UNMT models that share the same translation task but differ in an auxiliary language, inducing structured diversity across models. We then generate pseudo-translations for the primary pair using token-level ensemble decoding, averaging model predictions in both directions. These ensemble outputs are used as synthetic parallel data to further train each model, allowing the models to improve via shared supervision. At deployment time, we select a single model by validation performance, preserving single-model inference cost. Experiments show statistically significant improvements over single-model UNMT baselines, with mean gains of 1.7 chrF when translating from English and 0.67 chrF when translating into English.

摘要：我們提出了一個基於集成的自我訓練框架，用於無監督神經機器翻譯（UNMT）。從一對主要語言開始，我們訓練多個UNMT模型，這些模型共享相同的翻譯任務，但在輔助語言上有所不同，從而在模型之間引入結構化的多樣性。接著，我們使用詞元級集成解碼生成主要語言對的偽翻譯，對模型預測進行雙向平均。這些集成輸出被用作合成平行數據，以進一步訓練每個模型，讓模型通過共享監督來改進。在部署時，我們根據驗證性能選擇一個單一模型，保持單模型推斷成本。實驗顯示，相較於單模型UNMT基準，統計上顯著提高，從英語翻譯的平均增益為1.7 chrF，翻譯成英語的平均增益為0.67 chrF。

##### **Large Reasoning Models Struggle to Transfer Parametric Knowledge Across Scripts**
2603.17070v1 by Lucas Bandarkar, Alan Ansell, Trevor Cohn

In this work, we analyze shortcomings in cross-lingual knowledge transfer in large, modern reasoning LLMs. We demonstrate that the perceived gap in knowledge transfer is primarily a script barrier. First, we conduct an observational data analysis on the performance of thinking models on two datasets with local knowledge from around the world, ECLeKTic and MultiLoKo. Our regression analysis shows that script match - not language or family - is the primary predictor of knowledge transfer failure once model capability and question difficulty are accounted for. We further this finding by providing the LLMs with the key entities of the questions in their source language and find that this disproportionately improves cross-script questions. We then posit that these LLMs could be reasoning better at test-time. To evaluate this, we develop a synthetic generation pipeline to design SFT samples to encourage the model to better reason about transliteration ambiguities when trying to fetch parametric knowledge at inference-time. We show that teaching two models to reason better reduces the cross-script transfer gap. As a result, we conclude that there is potential to improve cross-lingual parametric knowledge transfer during post-training.

摘要：在這項工作中，我們分析了大型現代推理 LLM 中跨語言知識轉移的缺陷。<lb/>我們證明了知識轉移的感知差距主要是一個文字系統障礙。<lb/>首先，我們對來自世界各地的兩個數據集 ECLeKTic 和 MultiLoKo 中思考模型的表現進行了觀察性數據分析。<lb/>我們的回歸分析顯示，文字系統匹配——而非語言或語系——是知識轉移失敗的主要預測因子，當考慮到模型能力和問題難度後更是如此。<lb/>我們通過向 LLM 提供問題的關鍵實體及其源語言進一步驗證了這一發現，並發現這對跨文字系統問題的改善效果不成比例。<lb/>然後我們假設這些 LLM 在測試時可能能更好地推理。<lb/>為了評估這一點，我們開發了一個合成生成管道，設計 SFT 樣本以鼓勵模型在推理時更好地推理音譯歧義。<lb/>我們顯示，教導兩個模型更好地推理可以減少跨文字系統的轉移差距。<lb/>因此，我們得出結論，後訓練期間有潛力改善跨語言參數知識轉移。

##### **Evaluating Ill-Defined Tasks in Large Language Models**
2603.17067v1 by Yi Zhou, Basel Shbita

Many evaluations of Large Language Models (LLMs) target tasks that are inherently ill-defined, with unclear input and output spaces and ambiguous success criteria. We analyze why existing evaluation benchmarks and metrics fail to provide reliable or diagnostic signals of model capability for such tasks. We examine two case studies: Complex Instruction Following (CIF), where we identify recurring issues including limited coverage of real-world instruction complexity, sensitivity to instruction phrasing, inconsistent and non-comparable metrics, and instability introduced by LLM-based judges; and Natural Language to Mermaid Sequence Diagrams (NL2Mermaid), where we show how multi-faceted evaluation criteria can yield actionable insights beyond aggregate scores. Together, these case studies show that current evaluations frequently conflate distinct failure modes, yielding scores that are unstable, non-diagnostic, and difficult to act upon. Our findings expose fundamental limitations in existing evaluation practices for ill-defined tasks and motivate more robust, interpretable evaluation designs.

摘要：許多對大型語言模型（LLMs）的評估針對的是本質上不明確的任務，這些任務的輸入和輸出空間不清晰，成功標準模糊不清。<lb/>我們分析了為什麼現有的評估基準和指標未能為這類任務提供可靠或診斷性的模型能力信號。<lb/>我們檢視了兩個案例研究：複雜指令遵循（CIF），在這裡我們識別出重複出現的問題，包括對現實世界指令複雜性的覆蓋有限、對指令措辭的敏感性、不一致且無法比較的指標，以及由LLM基礎的評判者引入的不穩定性；以及自然語言到美人魚序列圖（NL2Mermaid），在這裡我們展示了多面向的評估標準如何產生超越總體分數的可行見解。<lb/>這些案例研究共同表明，當前的評估經常混淆不同的失敗模式，產生不穩定、無法診斷且難以採取行動的分數。<lb/>我們的發現揭示了現有評估實踐在不明確任務中的基本限制，並激勵更健全、可解釋的評估設計。

##### **Early Quantization Shrinks Codebook: A Simple Fix for Diversity-Preserving Tokenization**
2603.17052v1 by Wenhao Zhao, Qiran Zou, Rushi Shah, Yudi Wu, Zhouhan Lin, Dianbo Liu

Vector quantization is a technique in machine learning that discretizes continuous representations into a set of discrete vectors. It is widely employed in tokenizing data representations for large language models, diffusion models, and other generative models. Despite its prevalence, the characteristics and behaviors of vector quantization in generative models remain largely underexplored. In this study, we systematically investigate the issue of collapses in vector quantization, where collapsed representations are observed across discrete codebook tokens and continuous latent embeddings. By leveraging both synthetic and real datasets, we identify the severity of each type of collapses and triggering conditions. Our analysis reveals that random initialization and limited encoder capacity result in tokens collapse and embeddings collapse. Building on these findings, we propose potential solutions aimed at mitigating each collapse. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first comprehensive study examining representation collapsing problems in vector quantization.

摘要：向量量化是一種機器學習技術，將連續表示離散化為一組離散向量。<lb/>它廣泛應用於大型語言模型、擴散模型和其他生成模型中的數據表示標記化。<lb/>儘管其普遍存在，向量量化在生成模型中的特徵和行為仍然在很大程度上未被探索。<lb/>在這項研究中，我們系統地調查了向量量化中的崩潰問題，其中在離散碼本標記和連續潛在嵌入中觀察到崩潰的表示。<lb/>通過利用合成數據集和真實數據集，我們識別了每種類型崩潰的嚴重性和觸發條件。<lb/>我們的分析顯示，隨機初始化和有限的編碼器容量導致了標記崩潰和嵌入崩潰。<lb/>基於這些發現，我們提出了旨在減輕每種崩潰的潛在解決方案。<lb/>據我們所知，這是第一個全面研究向量量化中表示崩潰問題的研究。

##### **Do Understanding and Generation Fight? A Diagnostic Study of DPO for Unified Multimodal Models**
2603.17044v1 by Abinav Rao, Sujan Rachuri

Unified multimodal models share a language model backbone for both understanding and generating images. Can DPO align both capabilities simultaneously? We present the first systematic study of this question, applying DPO to Janus-Pro at 1B and 7B parameters under seven training strategies and two post-hoc methods. The central finding is negative: generation quality resists DPO alignment across all tested conditions on this architecture. No method improves generation CLIPScore at 7B (|Delta| < 0.2, p > 0.5 at n=200 per seed, 3 seeds); at 1B, all methods degrade generation, and the result holds across preference data types (real-vs-generated and model-vs-model) and the data volumes tested (150-288 pairs). Gradient analysis reveals why: understanding and generation gradients are near-orthogonal (cos ~ 0) with ~11-14x magnitude imbalance driven by VQ token count asymmetry (576 generation tokens vs. ~30-100 text tokens). This imbalance is the dominant interference mechanism in multi-task DPO; magnitude-balancing yields directionally positive understanding deltas (+0.01-0.04 VQA, though individually not significant), but the generation gap persists regardless. We identify discrete VQ tokenization as a likely structural bottleneck -- supported by the generation DPO loss converging to ln(2) -- and provide practical guidance for practitioners working with VQ-based unified models.

摘要：統一的多模態模型共享一個語言模型的骨幹，用於理解和生成圖像。DPO 能否同時對齊這兩種能力？我們針對這個問題進行了首次系統性的研究，將 DPO 應用於 Janus-Pro 的 1B 和 7B 參數，並在七種訓練策略和兩種後處理方法下進行實驗。主要發現是負面的：在這種架構下，生成質量在所有測試條件下都抵抗 DPO 對齊。沒有任何方法在 7B 下提高生成 CLIPScore（|Delta| < 0.2，p > 0.5，n=200 每種子，3 種子）；在 1B 下，所有方法都降低了生成質量，且該結果在偏好數據類型（真實與生成和模型與模型）及測試的數據量（150-288 對）中均成立。梯度分析揭示了原因：理解和生成的梯度幾乎是正交的（cos ~ 0），且由於 VQ 標記數量不對稱（576 生成標記對 ~30-100 文本標記），導致約 11-14 倍的幅度不平衡。這種不平衡是多任務 DPO 中的主要干擾機制；幅度平衡產生了方向性正向的理解增量（+0.01-0.04 VQA，儘管單獨來看並不顯著），但生成差距仍然存在。我們確定離散的 VQ 標記化是一個可能的結構瓶頸——這一點得到了生成 DPO 損失收斂到 ln(2) 的支持——並為使用基於 VQ 的統一模型的從業者提供了實用指導。

##### **Dependence Fidelity and Downstream Inference Stability in Generative Models**
2603.17041v1 by Nazia Riasat

Recent advances in generative AI have led to increasingly realistic synthetic data, yet evaluation criteria remain focused on marginal distribution matching. While these diagnostics assess local realism, they provide limited insight into whether a generative model preserves the multivariate dependence structures governing downstream inference. We introduce covariance-level dependence fidelity as a practical criterion for evaluating whether a generative distribution preserves joint structure beyond univariate marginals. We establish three core results. First, distributions can match all univariate marginals exactly while exhibiting substantially different dependence structures, demonstrating marginal fidelity alone is insufficient. Second, dependence divergence induces quantitative instability in downstream inference, including sign reversals in regression coefficients despite identical marginal behavior. Third, explicit control of covariance-level dependence divergence ensures stable behavior for dependence-sensitive tasks such as principal component analysis. Synthetic constructions illustrate how dependence preservation failures lead to incorrect conclusions despite identical marginal distributions. These results highlight dependence fidelity as a useful diagnostic for evaluating generative models in dependence-sensitive downstream tasks, with implications for diffusion models and variational autoencoders. These guarantees apply specifically to procedures governed by covariance structure; tasks requiring higher-order dependence such as tail-event estimation require richer criteria.

摘要：最近在生成式人工智慧方面的進展導致了越來越真實的合成數據，但評估標準仍然專注於邊際分佈匹配。雖然這些診斷評估了局部現實性，但對於生成模型是否保留了影響下游推斷的多變量依賴結構提供的洞見有限。我們引入了協方差級別的依賴忠實度作為評估生成分佈是否保留聯合結構的實用標準，超越了單變量邊際。我們建立了三個核心結果。首先，分佈可以精確匹配所有單變量邊際，同時顯示出實質上不同的依賴結構，這表明僅僅依賴邊際忠實度是不夠的。第二，依賴發散會在下游推斷中引起定量不穩定，包括回歸係數的符號反轉，儘管邊際行為相同。第三，明確控制協方差級別的依賴發散確保了對於依賴敏感任務（如主成分分析）的穩定行為。合成構造說明了依賴保留失敗如何導致錯誤結論，儘管邊際分佈相同。這些結果突顯了依賴忠實度作為評估依賴敏感下游任務中生成模型的有用診斷，對擴散模型和變分自編碼器具有啟示。這些保證特別適用於由協方差結構主導的程序；需要更高階依賴的任務，如尾事件估計，則需要更豐富的標準。

##### **HopChain: Multi-Hop Data Synthesis for Generalizable Vision-Language Reasoning**
2603.17024v1 by Shenzhi Wang, Shixuan Liu, Jing Zhou, Chang Gao, Xiong-Hui Chen, Binghai Wang, An Yang, Shiji Song, Bowen Yu, Gao Huang, Junyang Lin

VLMs show strong multimodal capabilities, but they still struggle with fine-grained vision-language reasoning. We find that long CoT reasoning exposes diverse failure modes, including perception, reasoning, knowledge, and hallucination errors, which can compound across intermediate steps. However, most existing vision-language data used for RLVR does not involve complex reasoning chains that rely on visual evidence throughout, leaving these weaknesses largely unexposed. We therefore propose HopChain, a scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop vision-language reasoning data specifically for RLVR training of VLMs. Each synthesized multi-hop query forms a logically dependent chain of instance-grounded hops, where earlier hops establish the instances, sets, or conditions needed for later hops, while the final answer remains a specific, unambiguous number suitable for verifiable rewards. We add the multi-hop data synthesized by HopChain to the original RLVR data used to train Qwen3.5-35B-A3B and Qwen3.5-397B-A17B, and compare against RLVR on the original RLVR data alone across 24 benchmarks spanning STEM and Puzzle, General VQA, Text Recognition and Document Understanding, and Video Understanding. Although this multi-hop data is not synthesized to target any specific benchmark, adding it improves 20 out of 24 benchmarks on both models, indicating broad and generalizable gains. To demonstrate that full chained queries are important, we replace them with half-multi-hop or single-hop variants, reducing the 24-benchmark average accuracy by 5.3 and 7.0 points, respectively. Multi-hop training also strengthens long-CoT vision-language reasoning, with gains peaking at more than 50 accuracy points in the ultra-long-CoT regime. These experiments establish HopChain as an effective, scalable framework for synthesizing multi-hop data that improves generalizable vision-language reasoning.

摘要：VLMs 展現出強大的多模態能力，但在細緻的視覺-語言推理方面仍然存在困難。<lb/>我們發現長 CoT 推理暴露了多樣的失敗模式，包括感知、推理、知識和幻覺錯誤，這些錯誤可能在中間步驟中累積。<lb/>然而，現有的大多數用於 RLVR 的視覺-語言數據並不涉及依賴於視覺證據的複雜推理鏈，這使得這些弱點在很大程度上未被揭示。<lb/>因此，我們提出了 HopChain，一個可擴展的框架，用於合成多跳視覺-語言推理數據，專門用於 VLMs 的 RLVR 訓練。<lb/>每個合成的多跳查詢形成一個邏輯依賴的實例基礎跳躍鏈，其中早期的跳躍建立了後續跳躍所需的實例、集合或條件，而最終答案則是一個具體且明確的數字，適合可驗證的獎勵。<lb/>我們將 HopChain 合成的多跳數據添加到用於訓練 Qwen3.5-35B-A3B 和 Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 的原始 RLVR 數據中，並在 24 個基準上與僅使用原始 RLVR 數據的 RLVR 進行比較，這些基準涵蓋 STEM 和 Puzzle、一般 VQA、文本識別和文檔理解，以及視頻理解。<lb/>儘管這些多跳數據並不是針對任何特定基準合成的，但添加它使兩個模型在 24 個基準中的 20 個基準上都有所改善，顯示出廣泛且可泛化的增益。<lb/>為了證明完整的鏈式查詢是重要的，我們用半多跳或單跳變體替換它們，分別將 24 個基準的平均準確率降低了 5.3 和 7.0 分。<lb/>多跳訓練還加強了長 CoT 視覺-語言推理，在超長 CoT 範疇中，增益達到超過 50 個準確率點。<lb/>這些實驗確立了 HopChain 作為一個有效的、可擴展的框架，用於合成多跳數據，改善可泛化的視覺-語言推理。

##### **Generative AI-assisted Participatory Modeling in Socio-Environmental Planning under Deep Uncertainty**
2603.17021v1 by Zhihao Pei, Nir Lipovetzky, Angela M. Rojas-Arevalo, Fjalar J. de Haan, Enayat A. Moallemi

Socio-environmental planning under deep uncertainty requires researchers to identify and conceptualize problems before exploring policies and deploying plans. In practice and model-based planning approaches, this problem conceptualization process often relies on participatory modeling to translate stakeholders' natural-language descriptions into a quantitative model, making this process complex and time-consuming. To facilitate this process, we propose a templated workflow that uses large language models for an initial conceptualization process. During the workflow, researchers can use large language models to identify the essential model components from stakeholders' intuitive problem descriptions, explore their diverse perspectives approaching the problem, assemble these components into a unified model, and eventually implement the model in Python through iterative communication. These results will facilitate the subsequent socio-environmental planning under deep uncertainty steps. Using ChatGPT 5.2 Instant, we demonstrated this workflow on the lake problem and an electricity market problem, both of which demonstrate socio-environmental planning problems. In both cases, acceptable outputs were obtained after a few iterations with human verification and refinement. These experiments indicated that large language models can serve as an effective tool for facilitating participatory modeling in the problem conceptualization process in socio-environmental planning.

摘要：社會環境規劃在深度不確定性下要求研究者在探索政策和部署計劃之前識別和概念化問題。在實踐和基於模型的規劃方法中，這一問題概念化過程通常依賴於參與式建模，將利益相關者的自然語言描述轉化為定量模型，使這一過程變得複雜且耗時。為了促進這一過程，我們提出了一個使用大型語言模型進行初步概念化過程的模板化工作流程。在該工作流程中，研究者可以利用大型語言模型從利益相關者的直觀問題描述中識別出基本的模型組件，探索他們對問題的多樣化觀點，將這些組件組裝成一個統一的模型，並最終通過迭代交流在Python中實現該模型。這些結果將促進隨後的社會環境規劃在深度不確定性下的步驟。使用ChatGPT 5.2 Instant，我們在湖泊問題和電力市場問題上演示了這一工作流程，這兩者都展示了社會環境規劃問題。在這兩種情況下，經過幾次迭代和人類驗證與改進後，得到了可接受的輸出。這些實驗表明，大型語言模型可以作為促進社會環境規劃中問題概念化過程的有效工具。

##### **LLM NL2SQL Robustness: Surface Noise vs. Linguistic Variation in Traditional and Agentic Settings**
2603.17017v1 by Lifu Tu, Rongguang Wang, Tao Sheng, Sujjith Ravi, Dan Roth

Robustness evaluation for Natural Language to SQL (NL2SQL) systems is essential because real-world database environments are dynamic, noisy, and continuously evolving, whereas conventional benchmark evaluations typically assume static schemas and well-formed user inputs. In this work, we introduce a robustness evaluation benchmark containing approximately ten types of perturbations and conduct evaluations under both traditional and agentic settings. We assess multiple state-of-the-art large language models (LLMs), including Grok-4.1, Gemini-3-Pro, Claude-Opus-4.6, and GPT-5.2. Our results show that these models generally maintain strong performance under several perturbations; however, notable performance degradation is observed for surface-level noise (e.g., character-level corruption) and linguistic variation that preserves semantics while altering lexical or syntactic forms. Furthermore, we observe that surface-level noise causes larger performance drops in traditional pipelines, whereas linguistic variation presents greater challenges in agentic settings. These findings highlight the remaining challenges in achieving robust NL2SQL systems, particularly in handling linguistic variability.

摘要：穩健性評估對於自然語言到 SQL (NL2SQL) 系統至關重要，因為現實世界的數據庫環境是動態的、嘈雜的並且不斷演變，而傳統的基準評估通常假設靜態的架構和格式良好的用戶輸入。在這項工作中，我們引入了一個包含大約十種類型擾動的穩健性評估基準，並在傳統和代理設置下進行評估。我們評估了多個最先進的大型語言模型 (LLMs)，包括 Grok-4.1、Gemini-3-Pro、Claude-Opus-4.6 和 GPT-5.2。我們的結果顯示，這些模型在多種擾動下通常保持強勁的性能；然而，對於表面層的噪音（例如，字符級的損壞）和在改變詞彙或句法形式的同時保留語義的語言變異，則觀察到明顯的性能下降。此外，我們觀察到表面層的噪音在傳統管道中導致更大的性能下降，而語言變異在代理設置中則帶來更大的挑戰。這些發現突顯了在實現穩健的 NL2SQL 系統方面仍然存在的挑戰，特別是在處理語言變異性時。

##### **Demystifing Video Reasoning**
2603.16870v1 by Ruisi Wang, Zhongang Cai, Fanyi Pu, Junxiang Xu, Wanqi Yin, Maijunxian Wang, Ran Ji, Chenyang Gu, Bo Li, Ziqi Huang, Hokin Deng, Dahua Lin, Ziwei Liu, Lei Yang

Recent advances in video generation have revealed an unexpected phenomenon: diffusion-based video models exhibit non-trivial reasoning capabilities. Prior work attributes this to a Chain-of-Frames (CoF) mechanism, where reasoning is assumed to unfold sequentially across video frames. In this work, we challenge this assumption and uncover a fundamentally different mechanism. We show that reasoning in video models instead primarily emerges along the diffusion denoising steps. Through qualitative analysis and targeted probing experiments, we find that models explore multiple candidate solutions in early denoising steps and progressively converge to a final answer, a process we term Chain-of-Steps (CoS). Beyond this core mechanism, we identify several emergent reasoning behaviors critical to model performance: (1) working memory, enabling persistent reference; (2) self-correction and enhancement, allowing recovery from incorrect intermediate solutions; and (3) perception before action, where early steps establish semantic grounding and later steps perform structured manipulation. During a diffusion step, we further uncover self-evolved functional specialization within Diffusion Transformers, where early layers encode dense perceptual structure, middle layers execute reasoning, and later layers consolidate latent representations. Motivated by these insights, we present a simple training-free strategy as a proof-of-concept, demonstrating how reasoning can be improved by ensembling latent trajectories from identical models with different random seeds. Overall, our work provides a systematic understanding of how reasoning emerges in video generation models, offering a foundation to guide future research in better exploiting the inherent reasoning dynamics of video models as a new substrate for intelligence.

摘要：最近在視頻生成方面的進展揭示了一個意想不到的現象：基於擴散的視頻模型展現出非平凡的推理能力。先前的研究將此歸因於一種幀鏈（Chain-of-Frames, CoF）機制，假設推理是在視頻幀之間順序展開的。在這項工作中，我們挑戰了這一假設，並揭示了一種根本不同的機制。我們顯示，視頻模型中的推理主要是在擴散去噪步驟中出現的。通過定性分析和針對性的探測實驗，我們發現模型在早期去噪步驟中探索多個候選解，並逐步收斂到最終答案，這一過程我們稱之為步驟鏈（Chain-of-Steps, CoS）。除了這一核心機制外，我們還識別出幾種對模型性能至關重要的 emergent 推理行為：（1）工作記憶，實現持久參考；（2）自我修正和增強，允許從不正確的中間解中恢復；以及（3）行動前的感知，其中早期步驟建立語義基礎，而後期步驟進行結構化操作。在擴散步驟中，我們進一步揭示了擴散Transformer內部自我演化的功能專門化，早期層編碼密集的感知結構，中間層執行推理，而後期層整合潛在表示。受到這些見解的啟發，我們提出了一種簡單的無需訓練的策略作為概念驗證，展示了如何通過集成來自相同模型但具有不同隨機種子的潛在軌跡來改善推理。總體而言，我們的工作提供了一種系統性的理解，揭示了推理如何在視頻生成模型中出現，為未來的研究提供了一個基礎，以更好地利用視頻模型固有的推理動態，作為智能的新基底。

##### **Efficient Reasoning on the Edge**
2603.16867v1 by Yelysei Bondarenko, Thomas Hehn, Rob Hesselink, Romain Lepert, Fabio Valerio Massoli, Evgeny Mironov, Leyla Mirvakhabova, Tribhuvanesh Orekondy, Spyridon Stasis, Andrey Kuzmin, Anna Kuzina, Markus Nagel, Ankita Nayak, Corrado Rainone, Ork de Rooij, Paul N Whatmough, Arash Behboodi, Babak Ehteshami Bejnordi

Large language models (LLMs) with chain-of-thought reasoning achieve state-of-the-art performance across complex problem-solving tasks, but their verbose reasoning traces and large context requirements make them impractical for edge deployment. These challenges include high token generation costs, large KV-cache footprints, and inefficiencies when distilling reasoning capabilities into smaller models for mobile devices. Existing approaches often rely on distilling reasoning traces from larger models into smaller models, which are verbose and stylistically redundant, undesirable for on-device inference. In this work, we propose a lightweight approach to enable reasoning in small LLMs using LoRA adapters combined with supervised fine-tuning. We further introduce budget forcing via reinforcement learning on these adapters, significantly reducing response length with minimal accuracy loss. To address memory-bound decoding, we exploit parallel test-time scaling, improving accuracy at minor latency increase. Finally, we present a dynamic adapter-switching mechanism that activates reasoning only when needed and a KV-cache sharing strategy during prompt encoding, reducing time-to-first-token for on-device inference. Experiments on Qwen2.5-7B demonstrate that our method achieves efficient, accurate reasoning under strict resource constraints, making LLM reasoning practical for mobile scenarios. Videos demonstrating our solution running on mobile devices are available on our project page.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過鏈式思考推理在複雜問題解決任務中達到了最先進的表現，但其冗長的推理痕跡和龐大的上下文需求使其在邊緣部署中不切實際。這些挑戰包括高昂的標記生成成本、大型KV快取佔用空間，以及在將推理能力提煉成適用於移動設備的小型模型時的低效。現有的方法通常依賴於將大型模型的推理痕跡提煉到小型模型中，而這些推理痕跡冗長且風格上重複，對於設備內推理來說並不理想。在本研究中，我們提出了一種輕量級的方法，通過結合LoRA適配器和監督微調來實現小型LLMs的推理。我們進一步引入了通過強化學習對這些適配器進行預算強制，顯著減少了響應長度，同時保持最小的準確性損失。為了解決內存限制的解碼問題，我們利用並行測試時間縮放，在輕微的延遲增加下提高了準確性。最後，我們提出了一種動態適配器切換機制，僅在需要時啟用推理，以及在提示編碼過程中的KV快取共享策略，減少設備內推理的首次標記時間。在Qwen2.5-7B上的實驗表明，我們的方法在嚴格的資源限制下實現了高效、準確的推理，使LLM推理在移動場景中變得可行。展示我們解決方案在移動設備上運行的視頻可在我們的項目頁面上找到。

##### **MessyKitchens: Contact-rich object-level 3D scene reconstruction**
2603.16868v1 by Junaid Ahmed Ansari, Ran Ding, Fabio Pizzati, Ivan Laptev

Monocular 3D scene reconstruction has recently seen significant progress. Powered by the modern neural architectures and large-scale data, recent methods achieve high performance in depth estimation from a single image. Meanwhile, reconstructing and decomposing common scenes into individual 3D objects remains a hard challenge due to the large variety of objects, frequent occlusions and complex object relations. Notably, beyond shape and pose estimation of individual objects, applications in robotics and animation require physically-plausible scene reconstruction where objects obey physical principles of non-penetration and realistic contacts. In this work we advance object-level scene reconstruction along two directions. First, we introduceMessyKitchens, a new dataset with real-world scenes featuring cluttered environments and providing high-fidelity object-level ground truth in terms of 3D object shapes, poses and accurate object contacts. Second, we build on the recent SAM 3D approach for single-object reconstruction and extend it with Multi-Object Decoder (MOD) for joint object-level scene reconstruction. To validate our contributions, we demonstrate MessyKitchens to significantly improve previous datasets in registration accuracy and inter-object penetration. We also compare our multi-object reconstruction approach on three datasets and demonstrate consistent and significant improvements of MOD over the state of the art. Our new benchmark, code and pre-trained models will become publicly available on our project website: https://messykitchens.github.io/.

摘要：單眼3D場景重建最近取得了顯著進展。得益於現代神經架構和大規模數據，最近的方法在從單張圖像中進行深度估計方面達到了高性能。與此同時，將常見場景重建並分解為單個3D物體仍然是一個艱巨的挑戰，因為物體的多樣性、頻繁的遮擋和複雜的物體關係。值得注意的是，除了對單個物體的形狀和姿態估計之外，機器人和動畫的應用需要物理上合理的場景重建，其中物體遵循非穿透和現實接觸的物理原則。在這項工作中，我們沿著兩個方向推進物體級場景重建。首先，我們介紹了MessyKitchens，一個新的數據集，包含現實世界的場景，特徵為雜亂的環境，並提供高保真度的物體級真實數據，包括3D物體形狀、姿態和準確的物體接觸。其次，我們基於最近的SAM 3D方法進行單物體重建，並擴展其功能，加入多物體解碼器（MOD）以進行聯合物體級場景重建。為了驗證我們的貢獻，我們展示了MessyKitchens在註冊精度和物體間穿透方面顯著改善了先前的數據集。我們還在三個數據集上比較了我們的多物體重建方法，並展示了MOD在最先進技術上的一致且顯著的改進。我們的新基準、代碼和預訓練模型將在我們的項目網站上公開： https://messykitchens.github.io/。

##### **ManiTwin: Scaling Data-Generation-Ready Digital Object Dataset to 100K**
2603.16866v1 by Kaixuan Wang, Tianxing Chen, Jiawei Liu, Honghao Su, Shaolong Zhu, Minxuan Wang, Zixuan Li, Yue Chen, Huan-ang Gao, Yusen Qin, Jiawei Wang, Qixuan Zhang, Lan Xu, Jingyi Yu, Yao Mu, Ping Luo

Learning in simulation provides a useful foundation for scaling robotic manipulation capabilities. However, this paradigm often suffers from a lack of data-generation-ready digital assets, in both scale and diversity. In this work, we present ManiTwin, an automated and efficient pipeline for generating data-generation-ready digital object twins. Our pipeline transforms a single image into simulation-ready and semantically annotated 3D asset, enabling large-scale robotic manipulation data generation. Using this pipeline, we construct ManiTwin-100K, a dataset containing 100K high-quality annotated 3D assets. Each asset is equipped with physical properties, language descriptions, functional annotations, and verified manipulation proposals. Experiments demonstrate that ManiTwin provides an efficient asset synthesis and annotation workflow, and that ManiTwin-100K offers high-quality and diverse assets for manipulation data generation, random scene synthesis, and VQA data generation, establishing a strong foundation for scalable simulation data synthesis and policy learning. ##### **SparkVSR: Interactive Video Super-Resolution via Sparse Keyframe Propagation**
2603.16864v1 by Jiongze Yu, Xiangbo Gao, Pooja Verlani, Akshay Gadde, Yilin Wang, Balu Adsumilli, Zhengzhong Tu

Video Super-Resolution (VSR) aims to restore high-quality video frames from low-resolution (LR) estimates, yet most existing VSR approaches behave like black boxes at inference time: users cannot reliably correct unexpected artifacts, but instead can only accept whatever the model produces. In this paper, we propose a novel interactive VSR framework dubbed SparkVSR that makes sparse keyframes a simple and expressive control signal. Specifically, users can first super-resolve or optionally a small set of keyframes using any off-the-shelf image super-resolution (ISR) model, then SparkVSR propagates the keyframe priors to the entire video sequence while remaining grounded by the original LR video motion. Concretely, we introduce a keyframe-conditioned latent-pixel two-stage training pipeline that fuses LR video latents with sparsely encoded HR keyframe latents to learn robust cross-space propagation and refine perceptual details. At inference time, SparkVSR supports flexible keyframe selection (manual specification, codec I-frame extraction, or random sampling) and a reference-free guidance mechanism that continuously balances keyframe adherence and blind restoration, ensuring robust performance even when reference keyframes are absent or imperfect. Experiments on multiple VSR benchmarks demonstrate improved temporal consistency and strong restoration quality, surpassing baselines by up to 24.6%, 21.8%, and 5.6% on CLIP-IQA, DOVER, and MUSIQ, respectively, enabling controllable, keyframe-driven video super-resolution. Moreover, we demonstrate that SparkVSR is a generic interactive, keyframe-conditioned video processing framework as it can be applied out of the box to unseen tasks such as old-film restoration and video style transfer. Our project page is available at: https://sparkvsr.github.io/

摘要：視頻超解析度（VSR）旨在從低解析度（LR）估算中恢復高品質的視頻幀，然而大多數現有的 VSR 方法在推理時表現得像黑箱：用戶無法可靠地修正意外的工件，而只能接受模型產生的結果。本文提出了一個新穎的互動 VSR 框架，稱為 SparkVSR，使稀疏的關鍵幀成為簡單而富有表現力的控制信號。具體而言，用戶可以首先使用任何現成的圖像超解析度（ISR）模型對少量關鍵幀進行超解析，然後 SparkVSR 將關鍵幀先驗信息傳播到整個視頻序列，同時保持與原始 LR 視頻運動的基礎。具體來說，我們引入了一個關鍵幀條件的潛在像素兩階段訓練流程，將 LR 視頻潛在信息與稀疏編碼的 HR 關鍵幀潛在信息融合，以學習穩健的跨空間傳播並細化感知細節。在推理時，SparkVSR 支持靈活的關鍵幀選擇（手動指定、編解碼器 I 幀提取或隨機抽樣）以及一種無參考的指導機制，持續平衡關鍵幀的遵循和盲重建，確保即使在缺少或不完美的參考關鍵幀時也能保持穩健的性能。在多個 VSR 基準上的實驗顯示出改善的時間一致性和強大的重建質量，分別在 CLIP-IQA、DOVER 和 MUSIQ 上超越基準達到 24.6%、21.8% 和 5.6%。這使得可控的、以關鍵幀驅動的視頻超解析成為可能。此外，我們證明 SparkVSR 是一個通用的互動、關鍵幀條件的視頻處理框架，因為它可以即時應用於未見過的任務，如舊電影修復和視頻風格轉換。我們的項目頁面可在以下網址訪問：https://sparkvsr.github.io/

##### **Chronos: Temporal-Aware Conversational Agents with Structured Event Retrieval for Long-Term Memory**
2603.16862v1 by Sahil Sen, Elias Lumer, Anmol Gulati, Vamse Kumar Subbiah

Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have enabled conversational AI agents to engage in extended multi-turn interactions spanning weeks or months. However, existing memory systems struggle to reason over temporally grounded facts and preferences that evolve across months of interaction and lack effective retrieval strategies for multi-hop, time-sensitive queries over long dialogue histories. We introduce Chronos, a novel temporal-aware memory framework that decomposes raw dialogue into subject-verb-object event tuples with resolved datetime ranges and entity aliases, indexing them in a structured event calendar alongside a turn calendar that preserves full conversational context. At query time, Chronos applies dynamic prompting to generate tailored retrieval guidance for each question, directing the agent on what to retrieve, how to filter across time ranges, and how to approach multi-hop reasoning through an iterative tool-calling loop over both calendars. We evaluate Chronos with 8 LLMs, both open-source and closed-source, on the LongMemEvalS benchmark comprising 500 questions spanning six categories of dialogue history tasks. Chronos Low achieves 92.60% and Chronos High scores 95.60% accuracy, setting a new state of the art with an improvement of 7.67% over the best prior system. Ablation results reveal the events calendar accounts for a 58.9% gain on the baseline while all other components yield improvements between 15.5% and 22.3%. Notably, Chronos Low alone surpasses prior approaches evaluated under their strongest model configurations.

摘要：最近在大型語言模型（LLMs）方面的進展使得對話式AI代理能夠進行持續的多輪互動，這些互動可以持續數週或數月。<lb/>然而，現有的記憶系統在推理隨著數月互動而演變的時間性事實和偏好方面遇到困難，並且缺乏對於長對話歷史中多跳、時間敏感查詢的有效檢索策略。<lb/>我們介紹了Chronos，一個新穎的時間感知記憶框架，它將原始對話分解為具有解決的日期時間範圍和實體別名的主語-動詞-賓語事件元組，並將它們索引在一個結構化的事件日曆中，與保留完整對話上下文的輪次日曆並行。<lb/>在查詢時，Chronos應用動態提示生成針對每個問題的量身定制檢索指導，指導代理檢索內容、如何在時間範圍內過濾，以及如何通過對兩個日曆的迭代工具調用循環來進行多跳推理。<lb/>我們在LongMemEvalS基準上對8個LLMs進行了評估，包括開源和閉源，該基準包含500個問題，跨越六類對話歷史任務。<lb/>Chronos Low達到了92.60%的準確率，而Chronos High則達到了95.60%的準確率，創造了新的技術標杆，比之前最佳系統提高了7.67%。<lb/>消融結果顯示，事件日曆對基線的增益達到58.9%，而所有其他組件的改進在15.5%到22.3%之間。<lb/>值得注意的是，Chronos Low單獨超越了在其最強模型配置下評估的先前方法。

##### **SocialOmni: Benchmarking Audio-Visual Social Interactivity in Omni Models**
2603.16859v1 by Tianyu Xie, Jinfa Huang, Yuexiao Ma, Rongfang Luo, Yan Yang, Wang Chen, Yuhui Zeng, Ruize Fang, Yixuan Zou, Xiawu Zheng, Jiebo Luo, Rongrong Ji

Omni-modal large language models (OLMs) redefine human-machine interaction by natively integrating audio, vision, and text. However, existing OLM benchmarks remain anchored to static, accuracy-centric tasks, leaving a critical gap in assessing social interactivity, the fundamental capacity to navigate dynamic cues in natural dialogues. To this end, we propose SocialOmni, a comprehensive benchmark that operationalizes the evaluation of this conversational interactivity across three core dimensions: (i) speaker separation and identification (who is speaking), (ii) interruption timing control (when to interject), and (iii) natural interruption generation (how to phrase the interruption). SocialOmni features 2,000 perception samples and a quality-controlled diagnostic set of 209 interaction-generation instances with strict temporal and contextual constraints, complemented by controlled audio-visual inconsistency scenarios to test model robustness. We benchmarked 12 leading OLMs, which uncovers significant variance in their social-interaction capabilities across models. Furthermore, our analysis reveals a pronounced decoupling between a model's perceptual accuracy and its ability to generate contextually appropriate interruptions, indicating that understanding-centric metrics alone are insufficient to characterize conversational social competence. More encouragingly, these diagnostics from SocialOmni yield actionable signals for bridging the perception-interaction divide in future OLMs.

摘要：全模態大型語言模型（OLMs）透過原生整合音頻、視覺和文本，重新定義了人機互動。然後，現有的OLM基準仍然固定於靜態、以準確性為中心的任務，這在評估社交互動性方面留下了重要的空白，這是導航自然對話中動態提示的基本能力。為此，我們提出了SocialOmni，一個全面的基準，實現了對這種對話互動性的評估，涵蓋三個核心維度：（i）講者分離和識別（誰在講話），（ii）插話時機控制（何時插話），以及（iii）自然插話生成（如何措辭插話）。SocialOmni包含2,000個感知樣本和一組經過質量控制的診斷集，該集包含209個互動生成實例，並具有嚴格的時間和上下文限制，並輔以受控的音視覺不一致場景以測試模型的穩健性。我們對12個領先的OLM進行了基準測試，揭示了它們在社交互動能力上的顯著差異。此外，我們的分析顯示模型的感知準確性與其生成上下文適當插話的能力之間存在明顯的脫鉤，這表明僅僅依賴理解為中心的指標不足以表徵對話社交能力。更令人鼓舞的是，來自SocialOmni的這些診斷提供了可行的信號，以縮小未來OLM中的感知與互動之間的鴻溝。

##### **SOMA: Unifying Parametric Human Body Models**
2603.16858v1 by Jun Saito, Jiefeng Li, Michael de Ruyter, Miguel Guerrero, Edy Lim, Ehsan Hassani, Roger Blanco Ribera, Hyejin Moon, Magdalena Dadela, Marco Di Lucca, Qiao Wang, Xueting Li, Jan Kautz, Simon Yuen, Umar Iqbal

Parametric human body models are foundational to human reconstruction, animation, and simulation, yet they remain mutually incompatible: SMPL, SMPL-X, MHR, Anny, and related models each diverge in mesh topology, skeletal structure, shape parameterization, and unit convention, making it impractical to exploit their complementary strengths within a single pipeline. We present SOMA, a unified body layer that bridges these heterogeneous representations through three abstraction layers. Mesh topology abstraction maps any source model's identity to a shared canonical mesh in constant time per vertex. Skeletal abstraction recovers a full set of identity-adapted joint transforms from any body shape, whether in rest pose or an arbitrary posed configuration, in a single closed-form pass, with no iterative optimization or per-model training. Pose abstraction inverts the skinning pipeline to recover unified skeleton rotations directly from posed vertices of any supported model, enabling heterogeneous motion datasets to be consumed without custom retargeting. Together, these layers reduce the $O(M^2)$ per-pair adapter problem to $O(M)$ single-backend connectors, letting practitioners freely mix identity sources and pose data at inference time. The entire pipeline is fully differentiable end-to-end and GPU-accelerated via NVIDIA-Warp.

摘要：參數化人體模型是人體重建、動畫和模擬的基礎，但它們仍然互不兼容：SMPL、SMPL-X、MHR、Anny及相關模型在網格拓撲、骨骼結構、形狀參數化和單位約定上各有不同，使得在單一流程中利用其互補優勢變得不切實際。我們提出了SOMA，一個統一的身體層，通過三個抽象層來橋接這些異質表示。網格拓撲抽象將任何源模型的身份映射到共享的標準網格，每個頂點的映射時間是恆定的。骨骼抽象從任何人體形狀中恢復一整套身份適應的關節變換，無論是在靜止姿勢還是任意姿勢配置中，均可在一次封閉形式的傳遞中完成，無需迭代優化或每個模型的訓練。姿勢抽象則反轉了綁定流程，直接從任何支持的模型的姿勢頂點中恢復統一的骨架旋轉，使得異質運動數據集能夠在不進行自定義重定向的情況下被消耗。這些層共同將每對適配器的$O(M^2)$問題減少到$O(M)$的單後端連接器，讓實踐者在推理時可以自由混合身份來源和姿勢數據。整個流程是完全可微分的端到端，並且通過NVIDIA-Warp進行GPU加速。

##### **Online Experiential Learning for Language Models**
2603.16856v1 by Tianzhu Ye, Li Dong, Qingxiu Dong, Xun Wu, Shaohan Huang, Furu Wei

The prevailing paradigm for improving large language models relies on offline training with human annotations or simulated environments, leaving the rich experience accumulated during real-world deployment entirely unexploited. We propose Online Experiential Learning (OEL), a framework that enables language models to continuously improve from their own deployment experience. OEL operates in two stages: first, transferable experiential knowledge is extracted and accumulated from interaction trajectories collected on the user side; second, this knowledge is consolidated into model parameters via on-policy context distillation, requiring no access to the user-side environment. The two stages are iterated to form an online learning loop, where the improved model collects higher-quality trajectories that yield richer experiential knowledge for subsequent rounds. We evaluate OEL on text-based game environments across multiple model scales and both thinking and non-thinking variants. OEL achieves consistent improvements over successive iterations, enhancing both task accuracy and token efficiency while preserving out-of-distribution performance. Our analysis further shows that extracted experiential knowledge is significantly more effective than raw trajectories, and that on-policy consistency between the knowledge source and the policy model is critical for effective learning.

摘要：目前改善大型語言模型的主流範式依賴於使用人類標註或模擬環境的離線訓練，完全未利用在真實世界部署中積累的豐富經驗。我們提出了在線經驗學習（OEL），這是一個使語言模型能夠從自身部署經驗中持續改進的框架。OEL運作分為兩個階段：首先，從用戶端收集的交互軌跡中提取並累積可轉移的經驗知識；其次，通過政策內上下文蒸餾將這些知識整合到模型參數中，無需訪問用戶端環境。這兩個階段反覆迭代，形成一個在線學習循環，改進後的模型收集更高質量的軌跡，從而為後續輪次提供更豐富的經驗知識。我們在多個模型規模及思考和非思考變體的文本遊戲環境中評估了OEL。OEL在連續迭代中實現了一致的改進，提升了任務準確性和標記效率，同時保持了分佈外性能。我們的分析進一步顯示，提取的經驗知識顯著比原始軌跡更有效，並且知識來源與政策模型之間的政策內一致性對於有效學習至關重要。

##### **Mediocrity is the key for LLM as a Judge Anchor Selection**
2603.16848v1 by Shachar Don-Yehiya, Asaf Yehudai, Leshem Choshen, Omri Abend

The ``LLM-as-a-judge'' paradigm has become a standard method for evaluating open-ended generation. To address the quadratic scalability costs of pairwise comparisons, popular benchmarks like Arena-Hard and AlpacaEval compare all models against a single anchor. However, despite its widespread use, the impact of anchor selection on the reliability of the results remains largely unexplored. In this work, we systematically investigate the effect of anchor selection by evaluating 22 different anchors on the Arena-Hard-v2.0 dataset. We find that the choice of anchor is critical: a poor anchor can dramatically reduce correlation with human rankings. We identify that common anchor choices (best-performing and worst-performing models) make poor anchors. Because these extreme anchors are consistently better or worse than all other models, they are seldom indicative of the relative ranking of the models. We further quantify the effect size of anchor selection, showing it is comparable to the selection of a judge model. We conclude with actionable recommendations. First, we conduct a power analysis, and compute sufficient benchmark sizes for anchor-based evaluation, finding that standard benchmark sizes are insufficient for pairwise evaluation and fail to distinguish between competitive models reliably. Second, we provide guidelines for selecting informative anchors to ensure reliable and efficient evaluation practices.

摘要：```
``LLM-as-a-judge'' 範式已成為評估開放式生成的標準方法。為了應對成對比較的二次擴展成本，像 Arena-Hard 和 AlpacaEval 這樣的流行基準將所有模型與單一錨點進行比較。然而，儘管其被廣泛使用，錨點選擇對結果可靠性的影響仍然在很大程度上未被探索。在本研究中，我們系統地調查了錨點選擇的影響，評估了 Arena-Hard-v2.0 數據集上的 22 個不同錨點。我們發現錨點的選擇至關重要：不良的錨點會顯著降低與人類排名的相關性。我們識別出常見的錨點選擇（表現最佳和表現最差的模型）實際上是劣質錨點。因為這些極端錨點始終比所有其他模型表現更好或更差，所以它們很少能反映模型的相對排名。我們進一步量化了錨點選擇的效應大小，顯示其與選擇評判模型相當。我們最後提出可行的建議。首先，我們進行了功效分析，並計算了基於錨點評估的足夠基準大小，發現標準基準大小對於成對評估來說不足，並無法可靠地區分競爭模型。其次，我們提供了選擇信息性錨點的指導方針，以確保可靠和高效的評估實踐。
```

##### **Internalizing Agency from Reflective Experience**
2603.16843v1 by Rui Ge, Yichao Fu, Yuyang Qian, Junda Su, Yiming Zhao, Peng Zhao, Hao Zhang

Large language models are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents that must plan, act, and recover from mistakes through long-horizon interaction with environments that provide rich feedback. However, prevailing outcome-driven post-training methods (e.g., RL with verifiable rewards) primarily optimize final success signals, leaving rich environment feedback underutilized. Consequently, they often lead to distribution sharpening: the policy becomes better at reproducing a narrow set of already-successful behaviors, while failing to improve the feedback-grounded agency needed to expand problem-solving capacity (e.g., Pass@k) in long-horizon settings.
  To address this, we propose LEAFE (Learning Feedback-Grounded Agency from Reflective Experience), a framework that internalizes recovery agency from reflective experience. Specifically, during exploration, the agent summarizes environment feedback into actionable experience, backtracks to earlier decision points, and explores alternative branches with revised actions. We then distill these experience-guided corrections into the model through supervised fine-tuning, enabling the policy to recover more effectively in future interactions. Across a diverse set of interactive coding and agentic tasks under fixed interaction budgets, LEAFE consistently improves Pass@1 over the base model and achieves higher Pass@k than outcome-driven baselines (GRPO) and experience-based methods such as Early Experience, with gains of up to 14% on Pass@128.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被用作自主代理，必須通過與提供豐富反饋的環境進行長期互動來計劃、行動和從錯誤中恢復。然而，現行的以結果為導向的後訓練方法（例如，帶有可驗證獎勵的強化學習）主要優化最終成功信號，導致豐富的環境反饋未被充分利用。因此，它們往往導致分佈收斂：政策在重現一組狹窄的已成功行為方面變得更好，但未能改善擴展問題解決能力所需的基於反饋的代理（例如，Pass@k）在長期設置中的表現。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了LEAFE（從反思經驗中學習基於反饋的代理），這是一個內化從反思經驗中恢復代理的框架。具體而言，在探索過程中，代理將環境反饋總結為可行的經驗，回溯到早期的決策點，並探索具有修訂行動的替代分支。然後，我們通過監督微調將這些基於經驗的修正提煉到模型中，使政策在未來的互動中能夠更有效地恢復。在固定互動預算下的多樣化互動編碼和代理任務中，LEAFE始終提高了相較於基準模型的Pass@1，並在Pass@k上達到了高於以結果為導向的基準（GRPO）和基於經驗的方法（如早期經驗）的表現，在Pass@128上獲得了高達14%的增益。
